Franco-Polish Talks Far from Understanding

Solidarity of the Little Entente Strengthened

(Geneva) After the settlement of the Saar issue, the hopes that have arisen from all sides were freely expressed yesterday when representatives of various countries exchanged views at the meeting of the Council of the League of Nations. During these various private talks, the issue of Germany's return to Geneva was also mentioned by representatives of various countries. In addition, the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact proposed by France has once again become the focus of discussion. French Foreign Minister Laval held lengthy discussions with representatives of the Soviet Union and the Balkan Entente last night. The governments of the Balkan Entente countries have already expressed their disapproval of this issue. (Havas, 19th)

A military newspaper in Warsaw expressed optimism about the talks between French Foreign Minister Laval and Polish Foreign Minister Beck in Geneva, saying that the talks between the two foreign ministers have been able to eliminate the differences between the two countries. Although the practical result of the talks between the two foreign ministers can only increase France's understanding of Polish principles, Poland views its policy as having won. The talks between the two are related to the Rome Accords and the Eastern European Locarno Pact. In other words, the political foundation for resolving the Eastern European issue must take into account Poland's interests. Polish Foreign Minister has repeatedly stated this solemnly, so this point must be included in any discussion of the Eastern European issue. If this can be achieved, Poland will take a positive attitude towards various agreements. (National News Agency, 18th)

A semi-official Polish newspaper in Warsaw today prominently published a Geneva dispatch, saying that it has learned from well-informed sources that the Eastern European Pact issue was not mentioned in the Geneva negotiations, and headlined it "Stalemate of the Eastern European Pact." Although the telegram is very vague, political circles in Warsaw believe that this is the result of talks between Laval and Beck. If so, the French newspaper's Geneva dispatch, which stated that Poland has not changed its refusal to join the Eastern European Locarno Pact after negotiating with French Foreign Minister Laval, seems to have been confirmed. (National News Agency, 18th)

(London) According to the Daily Telegraph, after French Foreign Minister Laval discussed with the Little Entente countries, the Balkan countries, and representatives of the Soviet Union, many difficulties have been found in the Rome Accords regarding the non-interference pact in the Danube region. The countries contacted by the French Foreign Minister have not yet agreed, as the foreign ministers of the three Little Entente countries have already issued a protocol stipulating that the Little Entente countries or the Balkan countries will not participate in the Danube Pact unless Laval can conclude a cooperation treaty with the Soviet Union when Germany or Poland refuses to sign the Eastern European Pact. The Little Entente and the Balkan countries also reserve the right to decide how to participate in the Danube Pact, and it is heard that Litvinov also holds the same attitude. All countries must give Laval a firm guarantee before Prime Minister Flandin goes to London. This proves the unity between the Soviet Union, the Little Entente, and the Balkan countries, so Laval must make a decision in Geneva. (National News Agency, 19th)

(Geneva) Representatives of the four Balkan Entente countries (namely Greece, Turkey, Romania, and Yugoslavia) recently held a meeting here, chaired by Greek Foreign Minister Maximos. No communique was issued after the meeting, but the meeting recognized the benefits of expanding the Rome Accords and advocated the establishment of broad understanding, which would not harm the proposal of the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. The Balkan Entente meeting was very satisfied with the speech of French Foreign Minister Laval at the Council of the League of Nations yesterday. (Havas, 18th)

Council Meeting of League of Nations May Conclude Today or Tomorrow 31

Discussing Minority Issues

Polish Representative Avoids Attending

Italian-Abyssinian Dispute Resolved Amicably

Difficulties in Resolving Iranian-Iraqi Border Dispute

(London) The current session of the Council of the League of Nations is coming to an end. If no unexpected events occur, Lord Privy Seal Eden can return to London from Geneva on the afternoon of tomorrow. (Havas, 19th)

(Geneva) In September of last year, Polish Foreign Minister Beck notified the General Assembly of the League of Nations that Poland would no longer cooperate with the committee appointed by the League of Nations to implement the guarantee of protecting ethnic minorities within Poland. Poland has long believed that the provisions on ethnic minorities in the Treaty of Versailles should be universally implemented and should not be applied exclusively to Poland and other countries, and cited the fact that Russia and Germany are not bound by this clause as unfair. At the time, European political circles were quite surprised. Subsequently, Poland made various arguments regarding the issue of ethnic minorities within Poland, but the reasons given were very weak. Poland apparently remains firm in its determination. When the Council of the League of Nations discussed this issue today, the Polish representative rose and left the room, only to return to his seat when the next issue on the agenda was discussed. (Reuters, 18th)

(Geneva) The dispute between Italy and Abyssinia will be negotiated directly by the respective countries in the hope of reaching a friendly solution. This was determined after French Foreign Minister Laval, British Lord Privy Seal Eden, and Italian representative Aloisi consulted last night. There is no need for the current session of the Council of the League of Nations to discuss it. (Havas, 19th)

(Geneva) An agreement in principle has been reached on the Somali border dispute between Italy and Abyssinia. The terms stipulate that the status quo remains unchanged. It is expected that the Council of the League of Nations will pass a resolution today to leave the issue for consideration during the next session. (Reuters, 19th)

(Geneva) Difficulties are currently being encountered here regarding the dispute between Persia and Iraq over demarcation of the border. The Council of the League of Nations is making efforts to mediate in order to seek a solution, but the attitude of the Persian representative is very strong. (Reuters, 18th)

(Geneva) The case of the dispute between Iran (i.e., Persia) and Iraq, which was originally scheduled to be submitted for discussion at the Council meeting of the League of Nations this morning, was not done so for some reason and will be changed to the afternoon. (Havas, 19th)

(Geneva) Efforts by the League of Nations to resolve the Somali border dispute between Italy and Abyssinia have also encountered setbacks. Supplementary Articles to Franco-German Agreement 33

Specifying Method for Coal Mine Redemption Payment

(Geneva) An agreement was reached between France and Germany yesterday on the issue of the aftermath of the Saar region, as reported in the previous telegram. After official publication, there are the following supplementary items. According to the agreement on the Saar issue concluded between France and Germany in Rome on December 3 of last year, the Council of the League of Nations registered it. This agreement has determined the most important principles, which stipulate that Germany should pay 900 million francs as a redemption payment for French state-owned coal mines. The payment method was specified yesterday. Germany will first pay France in francs circulating in the Saar region, and then remit in marks. Any shortfall will be paid annually at the price of coal produced in the Saar region, in installments over five years. In addition, after Germany recovers the businesses invested and operated by French private individuals in the Saar region, Germany recognizes its obligation to repay the capital invested by French private individuals, but the method of repayment is limited to when Germany has a trade surplus with France. Therefore, France and Germany must conduct more complete commercial negotiations. After joint decision by the two countries, all French economic relations will be negotiated directly by the two countries without the need for the League of Nations to manage them. The League of Nations will only handle the clearing of all past pending cases and the establishment of new systems. The German and French governments also pre-recognize that the resolutions of the Council of the League of Nations are of a mandatory nature and must be implemented. Finally, regarding the disarmament of the Saar region, Germany recognizes that the clauses on disarmament in the Treaty of Versailles apply to all other Rhineland regions, including the Saar region. (Havas, 18th)

Dutch East Indies Plans to Implement Foreign Goods Import Restrictions 40

Nagaoka Returns to Tokyo to Meet Hirota

Reports on the Progress of Dutch-Japanese Talks

After the Dutch East Indies government in Batavia declared its free trade policy on November 1 of last year, it formulated an import restriction order for fifty-six kinds of goods and an import permit system. At that time, as a result of Japan's serious protest, implementation was temporarily suspended. Now, the Dutch East Indies government still intends to announce this restriction order, planning to take the opportunity of the adjournment of Dutch-Japanese talks to announce and implement it. The contents of the new restriction order are as follows:

(1) The goods subject to the new restriction order reach more than sixty kinds, but due to administrative procedures, orders are issued in several batches, each time specifying five or six kinds. The first items to be restricted are glassware, porcelain, bicycles, and other items. It will take at least half a year to implement the restrictions on all sixty-plus kinds of goods. (2) The new restriction order does not apply to the quota system of various countries, with a few exceptions. Furthermore, the import quantity is based on the quantity needed domestically. (3) Restrictions on Japanese goods are based on the import situation in 1933, with 25% being the maximum limit. (18th Japan Associated Press Telegram)

(Tokyo) Nagaoka Haruichi, the Japanese representative who returned home due to the suspension of Dutch-Japanese talks, arrived at Tokyo Station at 9 PM last night and returned to Tokyo. (19th Dentsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) Nagaoka, the chairman of the Japanese delegation to the Dutch-Japanese talks, visited Foreign Minister Hirota at 11 AM this morning to report on the progress of the talks and to advise on the steps to be taken hereafter. Therefore, Foreign Minister Hirota decided to propose to the Netherlands to reopen the talks in the near future. (19th China United Press Telegram)

Famous American Aviator Lindbergh Prepares to Cross the Pacific 41

Establishing a Foundation for the Far East Air Route

(Washington) Colonel Lindbergh, a famous aviator, is currently in Miami City. According to his friend, once the trial of his young son's kidnapping case is over, Lindbergh will fly a "Clipper" aircraft to cross the Pacific Ocean, in order to establish a foundation for the Pacific air route. This Pacific air route is jointly operated by Watson Company and Pan American Railway Company, and is managed by Yang Ge, the former Director of the Aviation Department of the State Department. It is expected to open in April of this year, with the starting point being either Los Angeles or San Francisco, passing through the Hawaiian Islands, Midway Island, Wake Island, Guam, or Yap Island, and Manila, stopping at various locations, and finally reaching Guangzhou. Among them, the section from the United States to Hawaii is the longest, reaching 3,860 kilometers. The American female aviator Earhart recently flew this section in eighteen hours. If a "Clipper" aircraft is used, it will only take twelve hours. The entire journey from the United States to Guangzhou is 14,480 kilometers. Ordinary mail ships take four weeks, but after the Pacific air mail route is opened, it will only take sixty hours to arrive. (18th Havas News Agency Telegram)

Flemington Lindbergh has not given a concrete answer to the news from New York about opening a Sino-American Pacific air route this spring, and about his planned Pacific test flight. (18th National News Agency Telegram)

Surrounding Eastern Provinces and Japan, Soviet Russia Completes Far East Aviation Network 42

Seventeen Trunk and Branch Lines in Total

Used for Mail Delivery in Peacetime and Military Purposes in Wartime

According to information received by the Kwantung Army Headquarters in Shenyang from the China United Press, due to the slightly improved negotiations on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Russian-Japanese relations seem to have greatly eased. However, Soviet Russia's military preparations against Japan are becoming increasingly consolidated. Along the border line centered on Suifenhe, Hailar, and Manzhouli, Soviet Russia has deployed a large military force, and military supplies are being continuously transported by railways in the Far East. These land-based military preparations are being systematically prepared in conjunction with the Second Five-Year Plan. In particular, the expansion of the air force has been secretly carried out since 1932. Now, it has completed its aviation spider web in various parts of the Far East, that is, the trunk line connecting Vladivostok, Khabarovsk, and Moscow, with more than ten branch lines set up in the east, west, north, and south. Currently, these lines are used exclusively for mail transportation, but once war breaks out, they will immediately become military lines. It is found that the branch lines include the Aleksandrovsk and Yanuzhno lines centered on Vladivostok, the Hailar, Piyon, Komsomolsk, Okha, and Aleksandrovsk lines centered on Khabarovsk, the Pokzhi Gari Ao and Pok Yaer Ge Ao lines centered on Hailar, and the Tigas Dehli, Kerbin, and Geer Jiang lines centered on Nikolaevsk, totaling fifteen lines including other short lines. The flight status of these lines is extremely smooth, completely surrounding the northern sky of the Far East. In particular, the two branch lines centered on Hailar and Boli have very large transportation capacity. The North Sakhalin line between Okha and Aleksandrovsk also flies once a day or every two days, and this line and the Vladivostok line, together with the various lines gathered in the Primorsky Krai, constitute an encirclement line of the Japanese mainland, confronting the Vladivostok, Khabarovsk, Chita, and Moscow lines, completely surrounding Japan and the Eastern Provinces.

Foreign Aircraft Must Follow Prescribed Procedures When Passing Through Our Airspace 46

(Nanjing) After consultation between the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and military agencies, it was decided that when foreign aircraft need to pass through our country's airspace in the future, the ambassador of that country to China should fill out the application form in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs two months before the arrival of the aircraft and submit it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The aircraft can only enter our country's airspace after obtaining formal government permission. After entering the country, the aircraft must abide by the flight routes prescribed by our government and must not enter military restricted areas. However, if a foreign aircraft initially enters the country and accidentally enters a restricted area, the stationed area will notify the aircraft of the above-mentioned measures with a warning signal. The above-mentioned measures will be notified to the embassies of various countries in China for reference. (19th Special Telegram)

Academic Circles Strongly Advocate Caution Regarding Antiquities Being Transported to England for Exhibition 71

(Beijing) To celebrate the 25th anniversary of the coronation of the British monarch, the British government has requested our government to transport cultural relics collected by the Palace Museum and public and private sectors to London to hold a Chinese art international exhibition. The preparatory expenses will be advanced by the British side from China's Boxer Indemnity to England, and will be repaid from sales after the exhibition. Our government has agreed to the request, but Britain suddenly requested that the antiquities not be insured. The Palace Museum's antiquities are all priceless treasures of the world. If they are not insured, who can guarantee that nothing will go wrong after traveling across the ocean and being abroad for more than a year? Prominent figures in our country's academic circles, such as Xiong Fuxi and Zhang Xiruo, have expressed strong opposition to this and have specifically published their opposing opinions, hoping that the government will strictly limit the export of antiquities and provide high-value insurance. (19th Special Telegram)

Investigation of Kala-azar in Northern Jiangsu 114

Widespread Disease Area; Patients Totaling 100,000

Research Team Establishes Office, Provides Daily Treatment

Qingjiangpu Correspondence: Kala-azar is spreading in northern Jiangsu, with a very large number of sufferers. The most severely affected areas are east of Xuzhou, including Suqian, Huaiyin, and Lianshui. The Health Experiment Office of the National Economic Council organized a Kala-azar research team last year to conduct on-site investigations and establish an office to begin treatment. Recently, Chairman Chen of the Jiangsu Provincial Government has also paid extraordinary attention to this disease, sending personnel to Jiangbei to investigate and research in order to find ways to treat it, which is truly good news for those suffering from this disease. The distribution of Kala-azar in northern Jiangsu, the analysis of patients, the current status of diagnosis and treatment, and the details of the disease are described in detail below for the reference of those who are concerned about this disease. (1) Distribution of the Disease Area: Kala-azar, the English name for Kala-azar, is commonly known as 症塊病 ["Zheng Kuai Bing", roughly "lump disease"]. In the past, this disease was prevalent in the Mediterranean and India, and patients were all black-skinned and feverish, hence the name Kala-azar. This disease is rare in China. The black fever phenomenon that attracts attention is that the patient's spleen and liver harden into lumps, and the lump refers to the spleen lump. Kala-azar has only entered China for less than twenty years. At that time, a British soldier who had been stationed in India died in Beiping, and after autopsy and research by Xiehe Hospital, it was discovered to be Kala-azar. This was the first patient in China. From then on, it moved south and spread to Hebei, Shandong, Henan, Anhui, Jiangsu and other provinces. Although Beiping is the origin of Kala-azar in China, there are not many patients. Xiehe Hospital treats only forty or fifty Kala-azar patients each year. The most severely affected areas are along the old Yellow River channel. The number of Kala-azar patients diagnosed and treated by Qingjiangpu Renci Hospital and the church hospitals in Suqian, Xuzhou, and Suining are as follows:

Year 　1931　 1932　 1933

Qingjiangpu 3,383 people 2,904 people 2,200 people

Suqian ———— 350 people 650 people

Xuzhou ———— ———— 700 people

Suining ———— ———— 350 people

In addition, Donghai, Siyang, Huaian, Lianshui, Guanyun, Funing, Shuyang, Pixian, Xiaoxian, Fengxian, 𥓘shan, Peixian, etc., are also areas with a large number of Kala-azar patients. Taking Donghai alone, the number of patients exceeds 1,500. According to statistics, there are nearly 100,000 Kala-azar patients in northern Jiangsu. Qingjiangpu Renci Hospital treated a total of 2,904 Kala-azar patients in 1932. According to the analysis of the patients' origin, the numbers are as follows:

Qingjiangpu 881 Shuyang 390

Lianshui 1,287 Qiaoning 1

Xuzhou 2 Siyang 228

Suqian 3 Huaian 86

Guanyun 6 Funing 15

Donghai 2 Other 3

(2) Kala-azar Research Team: Kala-azar patients are mostly poor people. If new methods of injection are used, whether Tartanr Emali Neostan or Neostidoean is used, each person must spend at least 15 yuan. Poor patients cannot easily raise this huge amount of money. They often gather into fifteen people, each contributing one yuan to get fifteen yuan. A lottery method is used to decide who will use the money for treatment. Only one person out of fifteen can get the money for treatment, and the other fourteen can only sit and wait for death. Rural sorcerers take the opportunity to deceive people with lies, using sharp iron and porcelain objects to draw lines on the patient's abdomen to draw blood, claiming to treat the disease, but in fact, they are deceiving people for money, charging up to six yuan. The villagers are ignorant, wasting money and delaying treatment, which is the worst thing. In view of this, the Health Experiment Office of the National Economic Council organized a Kala-azar research team to conduct investigations and research in Qingjiangpu, and to provide treatment at the same time. The team is headed by Yao Yongzheng, Director of the Department of Parasitology of the Health Experiment Office, and Pu Nangu, Doctor of Medicine, is the Medical Director. There is also one medical officer, two technicians, one technical student, and two nurses. The Kala-azar Research Team arrived in Qingjiangpu in late April 1934. The office is located in the People's Education Center. They first started the investigation, and then started the treatment on June 31. Outpatient clinics are held every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday from 8:00 am to 12:00 pm. On Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, they go out for investigation. Those with severe illness or long distances can stay in the team, and food and drink are also provided by the team without additional charges. In terms of equipment, the Kala-azar Research Team currently has a registration room, an outpatient examination room, a waiting room, an examination room, a waiting room for injections, an injection room, a research examination room, an animal room, a drawing room, and an underground storage room. There are five microscopes, the highest magnification being 1,200 times. There are 430 voles, 15 rabbits, and many white flies. There are many hanging pictures and photographs on the walls. The equipment cost is more than 15,000 yuan, and the monthly use of Nootib'an is about 2,000 yuan.

(3) Analysis of Kala-azar Patients: The Kala-azar research team has investigated nine villages in Qingjiangpu and one village in Siyang. The investigation items are very detailed, including the number of households, patients, deaths, wells, ponds, pigs and dogs, and other health conditions and living environment, all of which are included in the investigation, and drawings are used to illustrate. The number of households in the ten villages and the percentage of patients are published below. (Liu Village belongs to Siyang, the rest belong to Qingjiangpu)

Spring Famine Feared in Jiangxi Province 115

Fields Untilled

Villages Prohibit Rice Exports

Nanchang Correspondence: Jiangxi Province was originally a rice-producing area. Before 1926, the annual rice exports from Jiujiang amounted to several million or even ten million yuan. In 1928, it also reached 8,493,154 customs taels. However, since the spread of the bandit scourge, over sixty of the province's eighty-one counties have been captured or partially captured by bandits. In these six years, the rural economy has been completely destroyed by the bandits. More than half of the rural able-bodied men have been drafted and died. Rice production, which is the center of the economy, has also been largely destroyed. The areas that have been fortunately recovered and are safe also have their production greatly affected due to the guerrilla looting by the Red bandits and the draft for joint suppression. Therefore, from 1930 to 1934, not only were there no rice exports, but Annam Saigon rice needed to be imported continuously to provide disaster relief. Especially in southern Jiangxi, there was an unprecedented rice shortage the year before last, with each dan of rice soaring to over forty yuan in silver dollars. As if misfortunes never come singly, last year there was also an unprecedented drought, with the entire territory suffering. Among them, northern Jiangxi was the worst affected. In the eighty-one counties, the average harvest of the upper and lower years, river villages, and mountain villages was less than 60%. A rice shortage occurred in various places where even the roots of the rice stalks were harvested. Due to the drought, it was difficult for one village to protect another and one township to protect another in the safe areas of the province. As a result, many places independently banned exports, while there was not a single grain left in the bandit areas and newly recovered areas, and people were crying out for food. Moreover, Ruijin, Ningdu, Yudu, Hengfeng, and even various bandit areas not only have no food, but even the seeds have been exhausted, and the fields are all barren, with lush grass up to the knees. Local accumulation societies are recruiting people to cultivate the barren land, but because the able-bodied men are listed as wounded, have fled, or have been coerced away by bandits, no one is interested. The Ningdu Rehabilitation Association has ordered the Baos and Jias to cultivate the barren land on behalf of the owners. Therefore, the food problem in the bandit areas is not just this year's famine problem. According to people who have traveled to the Fuhe and northern Jiangxi areas, the farmers who still have food to eat are estimated to be no more than 30-40%. However, there will be no grain to harvest until July, making this six-month spring famine a great calamity and difficult to overcome. In the past, rice prices in Jiangxi were always one, two, or three yuan lower than in Shanghai and Hankou, but now the price of rice in various places is over twelve yuan per dan, while agricultural products and their by-products have plummeted in value, and no one is interested in them. Therefore, the countryside can only accelerate its decline. The Civil Affairs and Finance Departments are investigating the food situation in various places to carry out adjustments to provide relief for the spring famine. The Four Provinces Farmers Bank is also transporting and selling food under the intention of the central government to adjust the food supply, as a drop in the bucket. (14th)

Definite Death of Xun Weizhou, Pseudo Army Commander of Anhui Bandits 116

Body Exhumed in Jing County

Head Cut Off and Displayed to the Public

Wuhu Correspondence: The bandits Luo Binghui and Fang Zhimin joined forces and fled to Anhui, but were fiercely attacked by the National Army and almost completely annihilated. It was found that these two groups were commanded by Xun Weizhou, the former pseudo 7th Army Corps Commander and later pseudo 10th Division Commander. The bandit Xun was only twenty-four years old, short in stature, and brave in combat. Last year, in the battle of Tanjiaqiao on the Yintun Road in southern Taiping, he was fiercely attacked by the Wang Yaowu Brigade of the National Army and almost completely collapsed. The bandit Xun, taking the lead, gave orders to the bandit crowd and was seriously wounded and killed by bullets. At that time, the Wang Brigade was making smooth military progress and advancing to pursue the bandits. Later, the Provincial Government Chairman's Office received information from Hu Yungen, the surrendered pseudo-Hygiene Minister, and Chen Daonan, the Management Squad Leader, stating that the bandit Xun was indeed killed in action in this battle and that they personally supervised the burial in Maolin Village, Jing County. In order to verify the confession, the Administrative Office ordered Zheng's Regiment of the 78th Division and dispatched Deputy Officer Du Jingtang and Wang Brigade Deputy Officer Huang Wenzhi to go with Hu Yungen and Chen Daonan to excavate. They were indeed exhumed in Pantun Tushan, three miles south of Maolin. The upper body was naked, and the lower body was wearing Western-style wool pants, a black-blue hat, and a red cloth five-pointed star hat flower. An examination of the bandit's corpse revealed a bullet hole in the upper part of the right thigh, and there were also scars on the arm. The neck injury was the most severe, presumably the fatal point. Deputy Officer Du and others cut off the bandit Xun's head and brought it back to report. In addition to displaying the bandit's head to the public, Liu Zhenhua also heavily rewarded the troops who fought in Tanjiaqiao to encourage them. (18th)

###驻军奋勇剿匪

Outstanding Achievements of the 468th Regiment of the 78th Division

绩溪通訊、陆军七十八师四六八团、原为十九路军改编、沪战时颇获荣誉、去年春、自闽调芜、适赤匪八九千众、窜陷太湖、该团奉命赴剿、规复太湖、乃赤匪侦知湖城兵力单薄、复以主力回窜、作复陷太湖之企图、该团团长符昭骞、尽率直属部队、星夜向太湖急进、始获不战而解太湖之围、又于十一月十五日、亲率步兵五连、及直属队一部、向古城以北冒险搜剿、刘主席以该团勇敢善战、威慑匪众、特拨二十余中队、归符团长统一指挥、后奉蒋委员长令调防、该团在驻皖剿匪期间、军纪颇佳、故离潜山时、围邑民众赠旗发扬、驻太时商民除赠旗犒劳外、复为　碑纪念、而刘主席倚畀尤深、赏责频颁、于奉命调防时、尤多方挽留、该团驻昌化旬日、除注意建筑防务、阻匪东窜外、复兴地方官民、致力于新生活运动、推进地方建设、孜孜不倦、夙夜匪懈、故于离昌时、该邑民众、亦赠旗褒扬、总计各县所赠该团旗帜、共有十幅、一般舆论、均谓为模范军团、（十九日）

Jixi Correspondence: The 468th Regiment of the 78th Division of the Army was originally reorganized from the 19th Route Army and won considerable honors during the Shanghai War. In the spring of last year, it was transferred from Fujian to Wu. At that time, eight or nine thousand Red bandits fled to Taihu. The regiment was ordered to go to suppress the bandits and recover Taihu. However, the Red bandits detected that the strength of the Taihu city was weak and fled back with their main force, attempting to retake Taihu. The regiment commander, Fu Zhaoqian, led all his directly subordinate troops to rush to Taihu overnight, and finally resolved the siege of Taihu without a fight. On November 15, he personally led the 5th Infantry Company and a part of the directly subordinate team to venture into the search and suppression north of Gucheng. Chairman Liu believed that the regiment was brave and good at fighting, and deterred the bandit crowd, so he specially allocated more than 20 platoons to be under the unified command of Regiment Commander Fu. Later, he was ordered by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to transfer defense. During the period of suppressing bandits in Anhui, the regiment had excellent military discipline, so when it left Qianshan, the surrounding people gave flags to promote it. When stationed in Tai, in addition to giving flags to reward them, merchants and people also erected monuments to commemorate them. Chairman Liu relied on them very much and frequently issued rewards and punishments, and made various efforts to retain them when ordered to transfer defense. During the ten days when the regiment was stationed in Changhua, in addition to paying attention to building defenses to prevent the bandits from fleeing east, it also revived local officials and people, devoted themselves to the New Life Movement, and promoted local construction, working tirelessly day and night. Therefore, when leaving Changhua, the local people also gave flags to praise them. In total, the regiment received ten flags from various counties. General public opinion said that it was a model army regiment. (19th)

Changzhou

Businessmen Kidnapped While Collecting Rent in the Countryside 119

Liu Hangsu, the second son of the late painter Liu Quran from Dongxiatang in Wuyi City, is wealthy and owns hundreds of acres of fertile land in Xizizhou in the third district. Liu Hangsu recently went to the island to collect rent rice and hired a boatman to accompany him. Spring Implementation of Cocoon Exchange Control 121

The Provincial Sericulture Improvement and Management Committee, in order to supervise the collection of improvement fees from various counties and to strictly enforce cocoon exchange control, has established a Wuxi office in this county, appointing Cai Jingde as director. In addition, Zhou Yuanxun, deputy director of the Yixing district, has been transferred to serve as the deputy director of the model district in this county. The committee also sent Secretary Guan Yida to Wuxi from the province the day before yesterday to visit Yan Shenyu, deputy director of the county's model sericulture district, Cai Jingde, Tang Xixiang, director of the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Station, and Ye Shaochun, chairman of the Cocoon Exchange Association, to discuss the implementation of cocoon exchange control. The results were satisfactory to all parties, so the implementation of cocoon exchange control in the spring is inevitable and considerable results are expected. Director Guan has now returned to the province to report.

Reaction to Changes in Business Tax Collection 122

The business tax for this spring recently received an order from the Department of Finance to shorten the collection period, setting the collection period for the first month of each quarter and ending it in the second month. Late payments will be subject to late fees, and businesses overdue for more than two months will be required to suspend operations. The county chamber of commerce reported that, according to past practice, the collection period was from the first month of each quarter to the last day of the last month, for a period of three months, which was extremely fair. Given the current drought, the decline of all industries, and the extreme tightness of money, paying taxes on a quarterly basis is already considered compliance with the law. It seems inappropriate to shorten the period to two months and impose penalties for late payment. Therefore, yesterday, a telegram was sent to the Department of Finance requesting approval to withdraw the order and continue to operate in accordance with the old regulations in order to avoid disputes. In addition, the county government issued a notice yesterday stating that rice shops, flower shops, wood shops, bamboo shops, and similar businesses must still pay business tax after paying taxes and obtaining licenses in accordance with the tooth tax regulations and must not avoid or take advantage of loopholes.

Abolition of Farmland Tax Collection Fees 123

Zhao Dihua, Director of the Department of Finance, recognizing that the accumulated problems in farmland tax collection in various counties in Jiangsu Province are deep and vary, and that a thorough reform is necessary to alleviate the suffering of the people and increase revenue, previously ordered all counties to earnestly rectify the situation. Now, in order to resolve difficulties and actively rectify the situation, it has been decided to abolish the principle of collecting all fees and expenses from the collection fee, starting in the 24th year of the Republic, and to set the following four measures: (1) The collection fee expenditure budget must be prepared and submitted early; (2) The collection fee income over the years should be submitted in detail in a list for review; (3) Collection fee income and expenditure should be included in the general budget; (4) If the collection fee is insufficient in a county, the county's various agencies should hold a meeting to discuss supplementary measures and submit them to the department for approval. Yesterday, County Magistrate Yan of Wuxi was instructed to conduct a detailed study and discussion immediately and to prepare a budget within ten days for approval.

Zhenjiang

"Hengyu" Ship of Zhenjiang Qing Class Robbed 124

The "Hengyu" ship of the Fu Huai Shipping Bureau's Qingjiang class, which was sailing downstream, was passing through the Qilipu area of Shiying Sishui Town at 8:30 PM on the 17th when six or seven bandits, disguised as passengers, suddenly fired shots into the air with pistols. Two bandit ships were lying in ambush at a nearby port connected to the lake. More than ten bandits jumped onto the ship and searched the purser's office and passengers, causing losses of over 3,000 yuan. While the bandits were searching the ship, the "Datong Huo" ship of the Qing class, which was also sailing downstream, arrived. The bandits fired shots again and boarded the ship to rob it, which lasted for an hour before they roared away into the lake.

Haimen

Young Girl Dies from Abortion 125

Chen Hongzhou's daughter, Zhenbo, a 17-year-old villager from the Rixin River area of the sixth district, was seduced by her neighbor Zhou Muyuan last autumn, resulting in a pregnancy. Zhou, fearing that the girl's father would find out, instigated Zhenbo to have an abortion on the 15th of this month. However, after taking the medicine, she suffered severe abdominal pain and unstoppable bleeding, and died the next day (the 16th). Her father discovered the truth and turned Zhou over to the township office for custody and requested the county government to investigate. After receiving the report, the county government sent Judge Chen to conduct an autopsy yesterday (the 17th) and confirmed the facts. The adulterer Zhou Muyuan was taken to the county and detained after a court hearing.

Land Dispute Leads to Tragedy 126

In Changlai Town, the third district, villager Peng Linfu wanted to borrow 50 yuan from his aunt Peng Shi by mortgaging 1,000 steps of farmland because his 70-year-old grandfather was bedridden and lacked medical funds. They were scheduled to sign the contract the day before yesterday (the 16th). However, when the time came, Peng Shi suddenly reneged, and the two sides began to argue. Linfu, unable to contain his anger, took a kitchen knife and砍 (kan, chop/hack) Peng Shi's head, causing blood to flow like a river and causing her to fall to the ground in pain. Neighbors who heard the commotion turned Linfu over to the district office and sent him to the county government for investigation. Peng Shi was carried to the county yesterday (the 17th). It is said that her injuries were severe and she may die.

Jiaxing

Case of Kidnapping at East Gate Cracked 127

The family of Lu Yubo, residing at No. 13 Zhou'anbang, Liuta Township, East Gate of Jiaxing, was visited by three bandits wearing blue short shirts and pants and carrying sharp knives at around 6 PM on January 15th. They kidnapped Yubo's second son, Laowu (in his twenties), towards the railway. Because Laowu refused to walk, the bandits hit his head with a brick, causing serious injuries. Finally, they killed him with a sharp knife and hid him in a tomb. The next day, Lu reported the incident to the Fourth Police Station for investigation. However, the day after that, the Lu family received a letter from the bandits demanding 1,000 yuan and arranging a meeting at Qixing Bridge on the 18th, with sugarcane and cigarettes as the signal. They reported it to the Public Security Bureau, and detectives disguised themselves and waited at Qixing Bridge. A bandit came to inquire and was arrested. He confessed that his name was Wu Er'a (aka Wu Yongcheng), residing at the home of Wu Peihao, Dalong, Jianqiao River, in this city. He also confessed that Wu Yongda and Wu Chengfa were involved in the kidnapping of Lu Laowu. The Public Security Bureau sent police to the home of Wu Peihao in Dalong and arrested Wu Chengfa and Wu Peihao. They confessed the details of Lu Laowu's murder and the hiding of his body in a tomb near Tanghui. On the 19th, the court was requested to conduct an autopsy, and a search was launched for the fugitive Wu Yongda to bring him to justice.

Naughty Child Plays with Fire, Burning Down Entire Village 130

The Xitangqiao Xiyizhuang in the fourth district of the county belongs to the Pang family in the city. The Zhuang is located in a remote area of the country and the houses are large and unoccupied. The Pang family assigned Si Zhang Lu Junlian to reside in the country to collect rent. Lu brought his son, Dabao, with him. Dabao, who is only five years old, was burning reeds in the wasteland outside the door the other day. The northwest wind was extremely strong, and the fire spread to the Pang family's Zhuang. Soon, it affected neighboring houses. For a time, smoke filled the air and the fire was fierce. Because the countryside lacked fire-fighting equipment, it was impossible to save the situation, resulting in the complete burning of all the nearby neighbors, causing untold losses.

Local News

Mayor Wu Expresses Opinion on Postponing the General Closing 136

One-sided advocacy is not enough to alleviate commercial difficulties

Deeply afraid that the impact will disrupt the market

Central News Agency reports that regarding the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation's proposal to postpone the current general industrial and commercial closing for one year and delay the payment of rent for six months, yesterday, this reporter specially visited Mayor Wu to inquire about his opinion. He gave the following statement: "In recent years, Shanghai has been affected by frequent disasters in various places and the decline of the rural economy. It has also been hit by the combined pressure of global financial and economic pressures. The economic downturn and the difficulties of various industries are unavoidable phenomena. However, recently, due to the efforts of all parties, the economic situation has become increasingly consolidated, and the social sentiment has become increasingly secure. In this environment of significant progress, if we want to gradually restore industry and commerce, we only need people from all walks of life to maintain and work together from the standpoint of the overall social welfare, and it will not be difficult to turn the tide. However, the development of industry and commerce should have basic conditions, namely, the protection of legal rights and the maintenance of industrial and commercial conventions. At present, the advocacy of postponing the general industrial and commercial closing and delaying the payment of rent for six months by some citizens are not in line with legal principles or human sentiment. This kind of one-sided advocacy is not only insufficient to alleviate commercial difficulties, but also may disrupt the market. It is not the way to prosper this city, and it is not what an orderly and disciplined society should have. This mayor cannot sympathize with it."

Japan Resolved to Invade Chahar 137

Japanese military publicly issued a statement

Chahar troops have minor contact with puppet troops

The External Affairs News Agency reports that Japan's attempt to invade Chahar has been a fact for two years since the fall of Jehol. At the beginning of the new year, Japan's position in the world fell into a desperate situation of international crisis, so it focused its diplomatic and military efforts on aggression against us. Military actions and diplomatic progress cooperated with each other. In diplomatic terms, people such as Suma and Luye were busy on the road between China and Japan. Suma was particularly active, even hurriedly touring various parts of Northeast and North China on his way to China. In military terms, the special meetings of resident military attachés held twice in Shanghai and Dalian in November last year and early this spring were particularly tense. Until recently, the Japanese navy and army stationed in Shanghai have repeatedly conducted armed exercises and parades, and in North China, they have found excuses to criticize the authorities of Hebei Province and directly provoked the Song Zheyuan troops in Chahar Province. Their evil intentions have almost become apparent. According to a report from Changchun, at 8:00 PM on the 18th, the headquarters of the Japanese Kwantung Army publicly issued a statement, claiming that they would attack our army in Jehol Province, and the wording of the statement about Song Zheyuan's troops was perverse and ridiculously sophistical. It can be seen that the denial of the tense situation in North China by the Japanese embassy in this port was just deceiving themselves.

The External Affairs News Agency reports from Beiping that the news that the Japanese army has been mobilized has been spread everywhere, which shows the tension in Chahar Province. The air force has already moved, and a large number of troops have been transferred from Gubeikou, Luanzhou, Kaiping, and other places to various places on the border of Jehol, including Guyuan. Because of the tense situation in Chahar, Song Zheyuan has sent Qin Decun back to Chahar to deal with it. Song himself is temporarily staying in Beiping because he still needs to meet with He Yingqin. Song told reporters that on January 13, the Chahar army and the miscellaneous troops of the puppet state had a small conflict in Zhangling near Guyuan in eastern Chahar. As a result, the invading puppet troops were repelled. As of now, the situation in Chahar is very peaceful.

The External Affairs News Agency reports from Beiping that according to today's news, the Japanese infantry stationed in Chengde was transferred to Daning and Daguzhen in western Jehol yesterday. Several Japanese aircraft have also been concentrated near Chengde. It is said that this action is the prelude to the joint expulsion of Song Zheyuan's troops by the Japanese and "Manchukuo" armies. The commander of the Japanese army stationed in Chengde recently sent an ultimatum to Song, urging him to withdraw his troops from Jehol as soon as possible. This ultimatum was conveyed to Song by the Japanese military attaché in Zhangjiakou. The Japanese officials in Beiping did not criticize this news, only saying that even if there is action, it will be limited to the local area. Daguzhen is 110 kilometers northwest of Chengde and only 80 kilometers north of Gubeikou.

Central Bank Loans Fully Repaid Yesterday 138

Money Market Eases and Foreign Exchange Rates Continue to Fall

Loans will continue to be issued if requested

In December of last year, the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications jointly prepared to release 10 million yuan in cash in order to meet the needs of the market and adjust the financial situation. Anyone with sufficient collateral could apply to the Central Bank for a mortgage, but it was limited to 100,000 yuan per household and stipulated that settlements were made every two days, and every Friday was a three-day settlement. Since the implementation of the loan, more than 50 banks and money houses have applied for loans, totaling more than 4.3 million yuan. After the New Year, the accounts have been returned one after another. Recently, the money market has eased, foreign exchange rates have continued to fall, and the market has become stable. As of the 19th, all borrowing accounts have been fully repaid. If there is a request for a mortgage, it will continue to be lent.

Net Profit of Two Railways Last Year 139

Totaled 3.02 million yuan

Issued a monthly bonus to employees

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, in order to issue bonuses to employees for the 23rd year of the Republic, specially instructed its subordinate departments and offices yesterday, saying, "According to the instruction No. 2626 from the Ministry of Railways on January 11, 24th year of the Republic, it is reported that the net profit of the two railways for the 23rd year of the Republic totaled 3.02 million yuan, and a request was made to evenly distribute the amount of one month's simple salary and wages to the employees of the two railways. After checking, the railway has a large amount of foreign debt, and it is still difficult to raise funds to repay the principal and interest on time. Considering the financial resources, the annual bonus should be stopped. However, considering that the employees of the two railways have worked diligently and selflessly for a year, they have made no small achievements. The various totals in the original calculation table are hereby approved for an annual bonus of one month's simple salary and wages to be granted as an incentive, so as to encourage the future. It is not allowed to be used as a precedent in the future. The rest shall be handled in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry's Instruction Nos. 2896 and 2897 of the 18th year of the Republic. As for the railway's accounting office's proposal to first issue bonuses to employees with monthly salaries of 100 yuan or less before the lunar New Year, and then issue bonuses to employees with monthly salaries of more than 100 yuan, it should be approved in order to adjust the financial resources, and no loans should be borrowed to increase the railway's burden. Except that we have already informed you by telegram, we hereby order you to comply with this order. In addition to distributing it to the various departments, we hereby urgently inform you of this matter."

Total Lunar Eclipse Last Night 146

According to the Shijie News Agency, Dr. Nagayama, Director of the Astronomical Observatory of the Imperial University of Tokyo, Japan, wrote a pre-discussion on last night's lunar eclipse, which is recorded for reference. Nagayama said that this lunar eclipse is the first since Showa 6 (Republic of China 20). The initial eclipse began at 10:53 pm on January 19, and the restoration occurred at 2:41 am on the 20th, lasting a total of 3 hours and 48 minutes. The total eclipse lasted from 12:03 am to 1:31 am, for a total of 1 hour and 28 minutes. During the eclipse, the moon will appear purple-copper red, because the atmosphere around the earth will be like a prism in a camera, transmitting only red light from the moon to the human eye. As for the cause of this phenomenon, it is because the earth travels between the sun and the moon. When the moon is totally eclipsed, sunlight cannot reach the moon, and the moon only receives light reflected from the earth, so people see it as purple-copper red.

Legislative Yuan's Notice of Reviewing Exchange Tax Arrives in Shanghai 147

Representatives of Five Exchanges to Go to Beijing on the Evening of the 23rd

Preparatory Meeting Held Yesterday to Discuss Key Points to Strive For

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits Petition to the Yuan and Ministries to Temporarily Suspend Tax Collection

According to the Dagong News Agency, the Legislative Yuan has scheduled a joint review meeting of the Finance and Economics Committees on January 24 to discuss the draft exchange tax law. The notice has already arrived in Shanghai, and representatives of the five exchanges have decided to go to Beijing on the 22nd of this month. A preparatory meeting was held yesterday to discuss various important cases and hold an expanded petition. The details are as follows:

Notice from the Legislative Yuan 148

To Whom It May Concern: The draft Exchange Tax Regulations has been resolved by the 85th meeting of the Third Session of our Yuan and has been assigned to the Finance Committee to jointly review with the Economic Committee. It is hereby scheduled to be held at 2:00 pm on January 24 (Thursday) in the meeting place of our Yuan. It is hoped that your association will send representatives to attend the meeting on time to present your opinions. Sincerely, Legislative Yuan Economic and Finance Committee, January 18, Republic of China 24.

Preparatory Meeting 149

The brokerage associations of the five exchanges, namely, gold, cloth, securities, flour, and miscellaneous grains, held a preparatory meeting at the Cloth Exchange at 5:00 pm yesterday. More than 20 people, including Wang Zhengzhuang, Xie Liansheng, Shao Wenmei, Zhang Weiyun, Xue Chengzhang, and Wu Limen, attended. Bian Futang, the chairman, reported on the Legislative Yuan's notification of attending the review meeting, and then the discussion began. (1) In addition to the chairmen and committee members of the five exchange brokerage associations being representatives to go to Beijing, additional representatives should be selected to attend the meeting for consultation. (Resolved) Each exchange should select its own representatives. (2) The central government should be requested to consider the difficulties of businesses and abolish the original tax collection plan. (3) Each exchange should collect various facts and materials regarding why the exchange tax should not be levied and contribute them for the authorities' reference. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 pm.

Scheduled Trip to Beijing 150

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, after repeated petitions from the exchanges, the authorities accepted the request and submitted it to the relevant committee of the Legislative Yuan for review. It is now heard that the review meeting has been scheduled for the morning of the 24th in Beijing. The five representatives, namely, Gu Xinyi, Chairman of the Miscellaneous Grains Exchange, Zhang Wenhuan, Chairman of the Securities Exchange, Wang Yiting, Chairman of the Flour Exchange, Xu Busun, Chairman of the Gold Exchange, and Mu Ouchu, Chairman of the Cloth Exchange, have scheduled to go to Beijing on the evening of the 23rd to attend the meeting and petition again. Yesterday, there was a rumor that the representatives had already gone to Beijing, which was a misrepresentation.

Petition from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 151

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, based on letters from the Shanghai Chinese Securities, Cloth, Flour, Gold, Miscellaneous Grains Oil Cake and other five exchanges, and the brokerage associations of each exchange, requesting to forward a petition to the Yuan and Ministries to abolish the collection of exchange tax, yesterday submitted a document to the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, stating (excerpt): It has been detailed in the letters from the brokerage firms to the Legislative Yuan and the Ministry of Finance last year and this time to the association members that the business of each exchange has been declining in recent years and it is difficult to bear the new tax burden. What the association wants to supplement and state is that although this exchange tax is taken from Japan's transaction tax, Japan only taxes futures transactions and does not tax spot transactions. Also, their tax amount is based on the difference between the buying and selling prices to prevent sharp rises and falls in the market, while we tax both spot and futures at the same rate, and the tax rate is higher than the Japanese system. All of this is not suitable for the current business situation in our country. Moreover, the main point of this case is not in this. Exchange tax is a type of behavior tax, and its nature is no different from the current business tax and stamp tax in various provinces. After the exchange completes the sale of goods, it is taxed separately with exchange tax, and there is no explicit exemption for other business taxes and stamp taxes that should be levied. In this way, the sale of goods must be taxed at least three times with a repeated behavior tax. In fact, for those that fall under the scope of business tax, one tax for wholesale and another tax for retail, combined with the exchange tax, will definitely be more than three times the tax. In this way, goods are taxed every time they change hands, which is no different from the fact that goods were taxed every time they passed through a place when the likin tax was not abolished. However, in the past, the tax was based on location, and now it is based on people. Therefore, before the system of repeated taxation is corrected, it is not appropriate to implement the exchange tax in a hurry. This is the general expectation of businesses. Furthermore, our country's tax rights do not extend to foreign businesses. Last year's National Finance Conference had a proposal to collect business tax from foreign businesses across the board, but it was not resolved due to the impossibility of implementing coercion. Chinese businesses in Guangzhou also expressed strong opposition to this matter, and the British even expressed their support in Parliament. In the end, the local Chinese businesses had no other choice. If the exchange tax is indeed implemented, it will also be a continuation of the business tax, only levied on Chinese businesses and not on foreign businesses, and the harm will be even greater. Foreign businesses in China only engage in wholesale and rarely in retail, and their territory is limited to treaty ports. Therefore, although the business tax is collected and exempted, it does not have a significant impact on the lifeline of commerce. As for the exchanges, they are the hub for leveling goods and have the ability to control the national market. No independent country would ever allow this power to be granted to foreign businesses. Now, because of the shackles of legal rights, we are powerless to restrain them and can only let them do as they please. Fortunately, the exchanges set up by Chinese people compete in the market, and their momentum has been slightly suppressed. In the future, if the exchanges run by Chinese people are successively subject to exchange tax, while those set up by foreign businesses cannot be taxed, people will be attracted to them like ducks to water. In this way, the ups and downs of the national market will be monopolized by foreign businesses. From the standpoint of the national economy, the disaster, which ancient people called floods and beasts, cannot exceed this. The state's tax revenue will not be enough to compensate for its losses. Therefore, before foreign businesses in China can be taxed across the board, this exchange tax should be delayed for the sake of reason and situation. This is purely from the standpoint of the national economy and is not just pleading for the exchanges. Based on the above two reasons, it is reasonable to submit this request to your Yuan and Ministries for review and approval, and to temporarily suspend the decision and implementation of the exchange tax law that is currently under review. This is in the public interest. Respectfully submitted to the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance.

Mingxing to Sail Tomorrow 152

Inland Transit Tax to be Exempted Soon

Shanghai-Ningbo Shipping Dispute Resolved, Sanbei Company Fulfills Agreed Terms, Renting New Ship Mingxing to China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Officially Opening Ningbo Route Next Tuesday. Yesterday, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has contracted the passenger tickets of the ship to Zheng Chengye, the comprador of Taikoo New Beijing. Mr. Zheng is scheduled to take over the ship tomorrow. Yesterday, Yu Qiaqing also negotiated the ship delivery procedures at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Mr. Yu has been painstakingly planning the Shanghai-Ningbo line, opening the Zhenhai inland port, so that goods can be duty-free in the future. The details are as follows:

Mingxing Officially Begins Service 153

The Sanbei Mingxing ship, after public discussion, will first be rented by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company for one month to replace the Xinjiangtian ship, which is undergoing repairs. The rent is 450 yuan per day. All salaries of crew members and sailors will be borne by Sanbei. Coal on the ship will be borne by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The rent for the first month, calculated at 31 days, is a total of 13,950 yuan. The second month will be re-rented by Ningshao Company for one month to replace the Xinning-Shao route. After two months, if the Yangtze River United Company is established, Mingxing will sail the Yangtze River. If it does not work out, Sanbei will run the Ningbo route on its own. The Mingxing ship will be rented by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company tomorrow, and will officially start sailing on Tuesday.

Zheng Chengye Contracts Passenger Seats 154

Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, originally intended to handle the passenger tickets of the Mingxing ship on a cost-plus basis. Looking around the bureau, Mr. Wu Delin is the most experienced and capable. It is most commendable. When the Mingxing ship starts sailing, it is planned to have Mr. Wu handle the passenger tickets. Mr. Wu is too busy with the public affairs of the business department to take care of this matter. Therefore, the passenger tickets of the Mingxing ship were contracted to Zheng Chengye, the comprador of Taikoo New Beijing, at a daily contract price of 1,150 yuan. A three-week trial run will be conducted first. Mr. Zheng has accepted and has negotiated a contract with the bureau yesterday.

Start to Eliminate Bad Practices 155

The deepest-rooted bad practices on the Ningbo route are the waiters' tips for drinks, which have the most adverse impact on passengers. Often, the ticket price is 3 yuan, and the waiters' tips for drinks also require 3 yuan. If it is a little less, there will be expressions of dissatisfaction. Various companies have repeatedly discussed reforms, but they have not been able to eradicate this deep-rooted practice. This time, the waiters on the Mingxing ship will implement a new system. The tips for drinks given to each passenger in the steerage class will be limited to one dime and a half to two dimes and a half, and no excessive demands will be allowed. The implementation of this new regulation breaks the decades-long practice of Shanghai-Ningbo ships and benefits the shipping industry.

Yu Announces Statement 156

Yu Qiaqing, General Manager of Sanbei, told reporters yesterday that the Mingxing ship's addition to the Shanghai-Ningbo route is purely to help the farmers of Ningbo, the second step is to help Ningshao Company, and the third step is to save the endangered shipping industry and recover a part of the shipping rights. Mr. Yu said that he has been planning this matter for six months and spent more than 400,000 yuan. A wharf has been built in Zhenhai, and a road has been opened to connect Ningbo inland. Ningbo is an important treaty port for the five ports of commerce. In the past, all goods entering and leaving had to pay customs duties. Zhenhai is an inland port. Once shipping is increased, Ningbo goods can use the road to directly reach Zhenhai to disembark and be treated as inland goods, which can be exempted from customs duties. Therefore, I opened the Mingxing ship to help the farmers of Ningbo. As for helping Ningshao, the opening of Mingxing will inevitably lead to competition. After the competition is formed, I plan to replace the Ningxing ship so that the agreement can still be signed and the Ningxing ship can be transferred to Ningshao to help its business development. The third step of saving the shipping industry is even more important.

Promote Tax Exemption 157

The government now exempts taxes on goods transported by trains, cars, and even civilian ships, but it still levies customs duties on goods transported by ships. For example, goods from Zhenhai to Shanghai can be duty-free as inland goods, but if the goods are transported to the northern and southern ports, they will still be subject to transit duties in Shanghai. This matter has been repeatedly contested with the government by all parties, and the request for exemption of transit tax on domestic goods has been approved by the central government. It is expected to be realized in the near future. This move will be of great benefit to the entire shipping industry.

Chairman Chiang Praises 158

Mr. Yu also said that when Chairman Chiang came to Shanghai this time, I mentioned to him during the audience that opening Zhenhai would enable the export of inland agricultural products to be exempt from taxes. Chairman Chiang praised this move greatly, saying that the recovered area of Jiangxi is planning to revive the rural areas. After the establishment of the Hangzhou-Jiangxi Railway, in the future, Jiangxi agricultural products can be shipped from Zhenhai and loaded onto ships. Therefore, the importance of Zhenhai port is the gateway to Zhejiang-Jiangxi shipping. It is predicted that Zhenhai port will become an important seaport in the future.

It is hereby announced that all customs brokers and businesses registered with this Customs must re-register in January of each year. It is hereby ordered that all such businesses must come to the Customs for re-registration before January 31. Otherwise, if it is found that the deadline has passed, they will all be treated as new businesses that have not been registered. This is hereby announced.

Rural Loans Difficult to Realize Temporarily 165

According to a certain private person, Mr. Xu once discussed this matter with the government authorities during his trip to Beijing last time. This is because the amount of money required for this move is huge and cannot be achieved with a small amount of money. Because the scope of the disaster area is too wide, there are nearly a hundred counties in a dozen provinces, and nearly a hundred villages in a county. The loan for farmers in one village is at least several hundred yuan. Extrapolating to a dozen provinces, the amount required is at least tens of millions, and at most tens of millions. This huge amount of money cannot be borne by the financial community at this time. Therefore, Mr. Xu's previous proposal of 30 million has been temporarily shelved. The only way to thoroughly relieve the rural areas is this. If money can flow back to the country, the rural revival is promising, and the national economic bottleneck can be solved easily.

Judicial Yuan Interprets Qualifications of Representatives of Trade Associations 169

The Judicial Yuan previously approved the Central Executive Committee's Mass Movement Guidance Committee's request for an interpretation of the eligibility of representatives and committee members of trade associations from the Jiangsu Executive Committee. The Council's Unified Interpretation of Laws and Regulations Committee has resolved the interpretation and replied by letter, which is recorded as follows: "If a company or firm sends representatives to attend a trade association, is elected as a committee member of the trade association, and is appointed by the trade association as a representative to attend the chamber of commerce, and the company or firm that originally sent him has closed down, according to the second item and fourth clause of the Revised Guidance Program for Mass Movements, the constituent members of people's organizations are prohibited from participating if they are not currently engaged in the industry. , his qualifications as a committee member and representative should be lost accordingly. This program was resolved on February 2, 22nd year. This Yuan's explanation No. 636 was December 10, 20th year. Before this program was resolved, if a businessman of a company or firm was appointed by the trade association as a representative to attend the chamber of commerce and was elected as a committee member of the chamber of commerce, and the company or firm had changed to another business with different characteristics and joined another trade association, although he is still engaged in commerce, he has changed his affiliation to another trade association and is not allowed to participate in the original association. His appointment to attend the chamber of commerce has also lost its basis. The spirit of the above program is that the qualifications of the representative and committee member should also be lost. "

Mr. Nie Lusheng Discusses the Reasons for the Failure of Cotton Mills 170

Burdened by Heavy Interest

Hopes for Government Interest Subsidies

The Guowen News Agency reports that in recent years, Chinese commerce has been affected by the global economic downturn, leading to a persistent decline. The situation is now particularly precarious, with bank closures, cotton mill shutdowns, and shop bankruptcies being heard of almost daily. Yesterday, the reporter specifically visited Mr. Nie Lusheng, a leader in the cotton industry, to inquire about new plans for the development of the cotton industry in the 24th year of the Republic. According to him, the reasons for the failure of the Chinese cotton industry are twofold: on the one hand, it is affected by the global economic downturn and the dumping of inferior goods; on the other hand, it is actually burdened by heavy interest. For example, cotton mills currently borrow a certain amount of money from banks, and the lowest interest rate is 0.9% per month, with some rates reaching as high as 1.1% per month, which is far higher than in foreign countries. Taking countries like the UK and the US as examples, the government provides meticulous protection for various industries. For instance, loans from national banks are interest-free, so factories can naturally strive for development. Looking back at our country, the opposite is true. Therefore, I (Mr. Nie referring to himself) hope that banks that already have dealings with cotton mills can form a banking syndicate and provide loans at lower interest rates, with the highest rate for cotton mills not exceeding 0.4% per month. If this is not possible, then the government should subsidize the excess beyond 0.4% to give cotton mills an opportunity to develop. In addition, experts in the cotton industry should be hired and sent to various cotton mills to investigate whether there are any shortcomings in the factory's work, with the aim of gradual improvement. Only then can the future of cotton mills be hopeful.

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Releases a Survey Report on Workers' Living Standards 174

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs has always paid close attention to the living conditions of workers in this city. The recently released analysis of the living conditions of workers in the city is particularly detailed. The average income for a family of five is approximately 416.51 yuan per year, while the expenditure is 454.38 yuan, resulting in a deficit of 37.87 yuan. The average percentage of families that need to borrow money to maintain their living is 88%, those who pawn items account for 78%, and those who participate in mutual aid societies account for 69%. Among them, those who live on loan sharking are the most miserable. Food accounts for 53.2% of the total family expenditure, rent accounts for 8.3%, clothing accounts for 7.5%, fuel accounts for 6.4%, and miscellaneous items account for 24.6%. Although food accounts for more than half of the expenditure, the nutritional components mainly come from plants, the quality is poor, and there is also a lack of quantity. Although the percentage of miscellaneous expenses is not too low, the proportion of unnecessary expenses, such as hobbies and superstitions, is too high, while education, hygiene, entertainment, and savings are too low. In large cities, the increase in living standards is actually faster than the increase in wages. Therefore, proper allocation of expenses is particularly important. If attention can be paid to this, the living conditions should not be so difficult.
