Employees Will Return to Work Today

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Shishi News Newspaper laid off a group of employees at the end of last year. The Shanghai Journalists Association held several emergency meetings on this matter and organized a special committee, sending representatives to negotiate with Zhang Zhuping, the general manager of the Shishi News Newspaper, multiple times. The issue has now been resolved, and the employees are scheduled to return to work today (the 20th). The letter from Mr. Zhang to the Journalists Association is recorded below: "Dear Sirs, since our newspaper stopped mailing, our business has been declining daily, and our income has also been dwindling. Our newspaper fears that if this continues, all employees will inevitably perish together. Therefore, we are temporarily implementing a partial downsizing to maintain the status quo. This was truly a last resort. Unexpectedly, this has led to misunderstandings. Representatives from your association have kindly come to discuss the matter in a friendly manner. All misunderstandings have now been cleared up. In this unavoidable situation, our newspaper is pleased to comply with your request and hopes that you will immediately inform the employees to return to work. Sincerely, Zhang Zhuping, January 19th of the 24th year of the Republic."

Lu Xihou Released from Prison Yesterday 187

After Posting an 80,000 Yuan Surety Bond

Lu Xihou, Chairman of the China Industrial and Commercial Bank, was approved for bail by the First Special District Court's Criminal Division on the 17th. However, Judge Yu Changzi, who was responsible for the liquidation process, placed Lu under custody. Yesterday, Judge Yu held another hearing to review the ordinary creditor claims (approximately 400,000 yuan). The representing lawyers Wu Peng, Wang Zhonghuan, and Tang Mingzhi all expressed hope that if Lu could be released, he could raise half of the 400,000 yuan within fifteen days. However, the court stated that since Lu's total debt reached over 940,000 yuan, although the creditor claims of over 400,000 yuan agreed to exempt Lu from custody, if Lu were to flee in the future, the remaining creditor claims would have no recourse. Therefore, it was ordered that Lu post a surety bond of 200,000 yuan to be exempt from custody. Lu's representing lawyers Wu Linkun and others stated that of the 900,000 yuan in creditor claims, excluding the 400,000 yuan in court today, 300,000 yuan belonged to Lu himself and 140,000 yuan belonged to the Siming Bank, with substantial collateral. Therefore, the amount of the surety bond should be reduced, as the 50,000 yuan bond paid to the Criminal Division could only cover creditor claims of less than 100,000 yuan. After Judge Yu considered this, he reduced the amount to 100,000 yuan. Lu claimed that in this economic downturn and at the end of the lunar year, it was impossible to obtain such a large surety bond. He requested that the amount be reduced to 50,000 yuan and that his three defense lawyers and eight or nine lawyers representing the creditors be jointly and severally responsible for the temporary guarantee before finding a surety bond. If a surety bond could not be found within three days, he would still be taken into custody by the court. Judge Yu then adjourned the court. After a detailed calculation of the accounts, he reopened the court and approved Lu to post a surety bond of 80,000 yuan. In addition to finding a new surety bond of 50,000 yuan, the remaining 30,000 yuan was approved to be added to the business guarantee provided to the Criminal Division. Before finding a surety bond, the creditor's representative lawyer and the defendant's representative lawyer were temporarily responsible for the guarantee. A guarantee letter would be submitted to the court within three days. Lu was then released from prison.

Bicycle Industry's Two Associations Petitioned Yesterday 188

Repair and Rental Industry Requests Public Utilities Bureau to Withdraw Order

Manufacturing Industry Convened an Emergency Meeting Yesterday

The Shiye News Agency reports that the two bicycle industry associations in this city, the repair and rental bicycle industry association and the manufacturing bicycle industry association, petitioned the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau yesterday, separately sending representatives to request the repeal of three issues: vehicle registration, stamping hard seals, and increasing the donation by one yuan. They also convened an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss solutions. The details are listed below:

Repair and Rental Industry's Petition to the Public Utilities Bureau 189

The Shanghai Repair and Rental Bicycle Industry Association submitted a document to the Public Utilities Bureau yesterday, stating: "We are submitting a document to report difficult circumstances and request changes to the measures in order to alleviate business difficulties and maintain operations. Since our association received the Public Utilities Bureau's Announcement No. 226 regarding the implementation of bicycle stamping procedures, we have complied with the order and notified all members to follow the procedures. Now, member companies have jointly submitted a petition, stating that there are many difficulties with the bicycle stamping procedures. We hereby present a detailed explanation to the Public Utilities Bureau: (1) Additional stamping. Bicycles are made up of various parts, such as the frame, handlebars, and wheels. Rental bikes are easily damaged, and the various parts are often exchanged and reassembled. The handlebars of bicycle A are sometimes installed on bicycle B, and the frame of bicycle B is sometimes installed on bicycle C. This kind of mutual assembly and complex circulation means that businesses renting ten bicycles must have fourteen or fifteen bicycles in order to maintain operations. This is because four or five bicycles are needed daily for repair and replacement. Once stamped, if bicycle A is damaged, the parts of bicycle B cannot be used for assembly, which will inevitably lead to a situation where circulation is impossible. The inconvenience is extreme. Therefore, the additional stamping point has practical difficulties and cannot be treated in the same way as privately owned vehicles. We should ask for a flexible approach to alleviate business difficulties; (2) An additional one yuan donation per year. Operating a bicycle shop is originally a small business operation, relying on this small profit to make a living. A donation of two yuan per bike is already a heavy burden. At a time when the market is sluggish, maintaining the status quo is already difficult. If the donation is increased again, it will be difficult to bear. We should ask for the repeal of the order and continue to pay the original donation to alleviate business difficulties." Based on this, the association has already convened an executive and supervisory committee to discuss the matter in detail. They all agreed that the stamping procedures have practical difficulties. Therefore, we are submitting this document to the Public Utilities Bureau for review, earnestly requesting compassion for business difficulties, and humbly requesting approval to repeal the order. This would truly be a benefit for both parties.

Manufacturing Industry Held an Emergency Meeting Yesterday 190

The Shanghai Manufacturing Bicycle Industry Association sent Mr. Wang to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau to petition yesterday morning. He was received by Mr. Xiao, a staff member of the bureau. However, because he did not get to the point, he resigned and returned to the association. The association convened an emergency meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon at the association's headquarters to report on the petition process and discuss countermeasures. Resolutions were made, but they will not be announced for the time being.

Xu Jianhou Accused of Embezzling a Large Sum of Money 191

More Than 20,000 Yuan in Banknotes Stolen

The Defendant Denies Everything

Xu Jianhou, from Dantu, is 24 years old. He used to work as a banknote counter at a certain bank. In May of last year, Xu suddenly left without saying goodbye. After an inspection by the bank authorities, it was discovered that Xu was suspected of embezzling 22,800 yuan in banknotes. They reported this to the police. Because Xu's whereabouts could not be determined, they requested the First Special Court to issue an arrest warrant and offered a reward for his arrest. It wasn't until 9:15 AM on the 17th of this month that Detective Wang Shenqing of the Municipal Public Security Bureau arrested Xu at No. 2 Baishou Lane, Penglai Road, Nanshi. He was taken to the Public Security Bureau for temporary detention. The day before yesterday, Chinese Detective Kang Zengxiang of the General Patrol Room went to take Xu back to the patrol room for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Criminal Division of the First Special Court for prosecution under Article 357 of the Criminal Law regarding embezzlement in the course of business. The defendant hired lawyers Dai Jien and Yin Jingxuan as his defense attorneys. Lawyer Wang Yaotang of the Public Concession Police then rose to state the facts of the case, saying that the defendant, Xu Jianhou, was a banknote counter. On May 17th of last year, the head of the bank's cashier department gave Xu 100,000 yuan in banknotes to count. According to practice, if the work could not be completed in one day, the banknotes would be locked in the drawer and the work would continue the next day. However, the defendant left the bank the next day and went elsewhere. It wasn't until June 2nd that he formally requested sick leave. The bank authorities became suspicious. Because it was close to closing the accounts, they conducted a detailed investigation and discovered that 22,800 yuan in banknotes were missing. However, because they did not know the defendant's whereabouts, the bank reported it to the police on July 3rd, requesting that the court issue an arrest warrant. It wasn't until 9:00 AM on the 17th of this month that Detective Wang Shenqing of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau was ordered to investigate the population in the area. When they checked No. 2 Baishou Lane, Penglai Road, they suddenly felt that the number of people in the house did not match. There was one more person than usual, named Xu Jisheng. He was taken to the Public Security Bureau and identified as Xu Jianhou, who was wanted with a reward. Xu Jisheng was his alias. The patrol room was notified to take him back. However, the defendant only admitted to 6,000 yuan at the patrol room, saying that it was all lost due to unsuccessful gold speculation. The patrol room is requesting that the case be postponed in order to clarify the truth. Zhu Peiqing, the head of the cashier department, then filed a complaint about everything. When questioned, the defendant stated that he had been working at the bank for two years. He denied all the facts stated by the patrol room lawyer and Zhu Peiqing, saying that because his salary was meager, he wanted to seek other developments. Therefore, he requested leave in May and returned to Huizhou to discuss investing and starting a business in Shanghai with his friend Hu Butang. However, after arriving in Anhui, the market was sluggish due to the Communist bandits' ravaging. Hu also had no intention of investing. Because of traffic interruptions, he did not come to Shanghai until January 2nd of this year. What I said at the patrol room was all forced and not factual, etc. Judge Qian Hongye verified the confession and ordered Xu Jianhou to be taken into custody. The trial was rescheduled for seven days.

Public Concession Health Conditions 192

The Health Officer of the Public Works Department's December report states that general health this month was good, as in the previous month, so both isolation hospitals were relatively idle, and the mortality rate was very low. The number of foreigners was 7.56 per thousand, the lowest record in history.

In December, one case of smallpox was discovered in the concession, the first discovery since September. The number of vaccinations decreased due to public relaxation and bad weather. However, this disease cannot be guaranteed not to occur again, so it is imperative that those who have not been vaccinated or have not been vaccinated in the past three years seek vaccination for protection.

This month, foot-and-mouth disease was found in livestock transported from the interior, and even in slaughterhouses. This disease did not previously exist in the concession. Now, in conjunction with the Veterinary Division of the Municipal Government and the French Concession, measures have been implemented to restrict imports, which may stop its spread. However, given the severity of the infectiousness of this disease, we cannot be overly optimistic. At the beginning of the month, about 25 to 30 percent of the cattle found in the slaughterhouse were infected, but by the end of the month, they were rarely seen. Presumably, cattle dealers have changed their purchasing locations.

Chinese residents reported 1,124 births, including 608 males and 461 females. As for the mortality rate, it was 9.58 per thousand, a decrease of 8.30 compared to the previous month.

This month, except for a slight increase in diphtheria among the Chinese, other infectious diseases were less prevalent. Sixty people sought treatment at the rabies clinic, of which fifteen were from other cities.

Regarding the health of schoolchildren, 463 students were absent from school due to illness this month, of which only 29 were due to infectious diseases. An ophthalmic trachoma clinic has now been established and is treating many students free of charge.

The average daily milk production was 33,865 pounds, an increase of 4.77 percent compared to the previous month. Two milk samples were found to not meet chemical standards, and five did not meet bacterial standards, all from Class B dairies. The number of slaughters this month decreased due to seasonal factors and increased livestock prices.

Gao Maogong, Strapped for Cash, Was Kidnapped in a Bizarre Incident 193

Factory Director Ma Rongguan Was Dragged Down

Mistress Shi Temporarily Leads the Investigation

Yesterday morning at 9:50, a kidnapping occurred near the Dada Rubber Overshoe Factory on Zhongshan Road North, Fanhuan Ferry, West Shanghai. The details are recorded below.

Employed as an Engineer at a Lime Factory 194

Gao Maogong, a native of Xinchang, Zhejiang, is 31 years old and resides at No. 12, West End, Zhongshan Bridge North, Fanhuan Ferry, West Shanghai. His wife, Wang, passed away more than four years ago. He has a son named A'da, who lives in his hometown. Gao, not used to living alone in Shanghai, cohabitated with Shi (named Lanxuan, currently 36 years old), a woman from his hometown whom he met two years ago. Gao originally worked at Kong Shiyang Foreign Firm. On September 1 last year, he was transferred to the position of engineer at Shunchang Lime Factory on Zhongshan Road. Because of his meager income, he was very strapped for cash.

Accompanying the Factory Director Out by Car 195

Since Gao joined the factory, he has been exceptionally diligent in his duties, and thus highly valued by the factory director. Yesterday morning, after Gao arrived at the factory at around 8:00 AM, the factory director, Ma Rongguan, needed to discuss business and instructed Gao to go out with him in Ma's private City License No. 1741, Concession License No. 4676 Austin car, driven by chauffeur Li Amao. They planned to go to an office in Chengde Lane, Gordon Road. Unexpectedly, when the car reached the vicinity of the Dada Overshoe Factory, four bandits suddenly appeared.

Dragged Ma Down and Drove Off with Gao 196

All four bandits were dressed in black, three holding pistols. Two bandits first rode bicycles and, seeing the car coming from the north, rode forward to block the car. The driver, fearing trouble, immediately braked. At that moment, two more bandits jumped out from the roadside and got into the car, dragging the factory director Rongguan down. The bandit driver drove south across Zhongshan Bridge and turned into Kaixuan Road. At the intersection of Daxi Road, the car slowed down, and the two bandits expelled the chauffeur Li Amao, driving west and fleeing. The two bandits on bicycles also fled without a trace.

Detectives Mobilized to Pursue 197

After the factory director Ma Rongguan was dragged down by the bandits, he ran to a nearby girls' middle school and used the telephone to report to the Caojiadu Branch Bureau. Director Wang received the report and immediately ordered Inspectors Yang and Long to lead all the patrol officers and detectives, including Squad Leader Geng Shouchun, Foreman Cao Chuqiao, Detectives Wang Yixin, Shi Yulin, Li Changfa, Zhang Shaoming, Zhu Bengui, and Zhang Wenbin to pursue in all directions. At the same time, he reported to Director Wen and notified all police stations to investigate.

Kidnapped Car Still Not Found 198

The entire detective team set out to pursue until evening, but there was no trace of them, and the car was not found either. The chauffeur Li Amao and Gao's mistress Shi were taken into custody. According to Li's statement, he is 23 years old, from Haizhou, and has been working as the factory director's chauffeur for more than a year. He described Gao's kidnapping in detail. According to Shi's statement, she is 36 years old, from Xinchang. She had previously cohabitated with Lü Zhongxu, operating a catering business on Zhongshan Bridge. After separating from Lü three years ago, she cohabitated with Gao. Her remaining words were evasive. Squad Leader Geng suspected her and took her to the headquarters for interrogation. It was then learned that she was naturally flamboyant and proficient in Japanese. She previously worked at the old Toyoda factory, a Japanese company, and now works at the new Toyoda factory as a clerk and translator, earning a monthly salary of fifty yuan. Nearby workers call her a female tycoon.

Dispute Arising from Trivial Matters, Judge Advises to Avoid Litigation 199

Plaintiff Accepts Advice

Both Parties Withdraw, Ceasing Dispute

Lu Xingyuan, former President of the Provisional Court and the Court of Appeal, has been practicing law in Shanghai since leaving office, collaborating with British lawyer Gao Yi to establish an office at No. 39 Beijing Road. Last year, due to handling a rent increase case for landlord against tenant Wang Xiqing, the case was litigated in the First Special District District Court. The first instance ruled that the plaintiff's request to increase the rent was insufficient and rejected it. Lawyer Lu, still representing the landlord, appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. On January 4, the Civil Division of the High Court summoned Wang Xiqing and others to appear for questioning. After the judge concluded the trial and announced the adjournment, Wang and others claimed that the remarks made by Lawyer Lu Xingyuan in court that day slandered the appellants. Therefore, they, together with other tenants Yuan Rongyi, Zhang Jingqing, Wang Shizhen, Wang Hu, Wang Meifang, Zhao Helin, Li Jitao, Shi Shouhong, Fan Dingzhang, Zhang Weixian, and ten others, filed a criminal self-accusation against Lu Xingyuan and Sun Guchen, who commissioned Lu to represent the rent increase, for obstructing their reputation, requesting that they be interrogated and punished according to law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng of the First Special Court opened the trial. Only Wang Xiqing, Wang Hu, Zhang Jingqing, and Zhang Weixian appeared as plaintiffs; the rest appointed Wang Xiqing as their representative. The defendants Lu and Sun both appeared. According to Wang Xiqing's statement, at the trial of the rent increase case in the Civil Division of the High Court on January 4, Lawyer Lu Xingyuan, as the representative of the appellant, stated to the court that the tenants could have increased the rent, but some tenants, as unethical elements, used the rent increase issue to solicit bribes of more than a thousand yuan from the landlord. If the landlord could sacrifice this amount of money, these unethical elements would have no objection. However, the landlord refused their request, so these unethical elements organized a tenant union to obstruct the rent increase and engage in sabotage, eventually leading to litigation. Lawyer Lu repeatedly said this argument up to five times. Who exactly are these unethical elements? Who solicited bribes from the landlord? Lawyer Lu should clearly announce and present evidence, and so on. Lu Xingyuan absolutely denied making such remarks, requested to obtain the record of the trial from the High Court, and specifically filed a counterclaim because Wang Xiqing's allegations were untrue. Sun Guchen claimed that he did not appear at the High Court trial and that the plaintiff's statement that Lawyer Lu's remarks were instigated by him was even more speculative. Judge Huang believed that since people were involved in litigation in court, it was inevitable that they would attack each other. This case arose from trivial matters, and there was no need for litigation. He then advised the plaintiff to withdraw the self-accusation. After the plaintiffs present expressed that they would not accept the advice, he turned to advise the defendant to also withdraw the counterclaim. Thus, both parties ceased the dispute.

The Shanghai South Shelter Requests Allocation of Cotton Clothing 200

Yesterday's Letter to the Provincial Drought Relief Associations

The Shanghai South Temporary Shelter of the Joint Association of Charity Organizations in this city is experiencing severe cold weather and an increasing number of people being sheltered. The existing stock of cotton clothing is insufficient for distribution. Yesterday, a letter was sent to the Drought Relief Associations of various provinces requesting donations of clothing to be distributed to help the poor. The original letter is transcribed as follows: "To the esteemed Associations, our shelter is housing poor people and unemployed workers at the Chaozhou Guild Hall and Chaozhou-Huishan Villa, totaling more than 2,400 people. More people are crowding in every day. All the cotton clothing donated by various charity organizations and philanthropists, including the amount saved from last year, totals less than a thousand sets, making it difficult to fully distribute to the poor and causing a great shortage. Moreover, our shelter has no fixed funds. In addition, the drought in various provinces last year was severe, and in recent years, rural areas have gone bankrupt and industry and commerce have declined, making fundraising difficult. The number of unemployed poor people is greater than in previous years. The weather is getting colder, and the number of people being sheltered is increasing. We are unable to purchase cotton clothing ourselves. Therefore, we are writing to earnestly request your esteemed association to grant assistance. We hope that you will donate some of the cotton clothing donated by various sectors to be distributed to the poor to help them through the severe winter and get through the end of the year. Your merit will be immeasurable."

Yesterday's Termination of Debate Was Revoked

Small Lumber Worker Crushed to Death 211

Zhang Xiugeng Brothers Carrying Lumber

One Slip, Eternal Regret

The laborer Zhang Xiugeng, 37 years old, from Taizhou, yesterday morning at 6:30, Zhang and his brother Xiufu were carrying a huge log together from the newly stacked lumber pile about ten feet high in the Shuntai Lumberyard outside the Youche Wharf in Nanshi, from the gangplank to the ground. At that time, Zhang's brother Xiufu was walking in front, while Zhang was in the back. Unexpectedly, he accidentally slipped, falling off the gangplank and onto the ground. The log he was carrying immediately fell down with him, pressing on Zhang's head. In an instant, his brains splattered, and with a miserable cry, he died. The lumberyard reported the situation to the Dongjiadu Police Station in charge. Upon hearing the report, the police station, considering that the matter concerned human life, instructed the local ward head to report to the Shanghai District Court and send someone to examine the body.

Robbers Come to Tax Collector's Home 212

Chen Boming, a tax collector from the South Shanghai Collection Office of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau, is from Zhejiang and lives at No. 124 Xintai Lane, Xintai Wharf, Shiliupu, Nanshi. His wife, Chen Lingxue, is currently a female inspector at the Inspectorate of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Yesterday afternoon at 3:50, four robbers suddenly broke into Chen's home, took out pistols, and warned them not to make a sound. They rummaged through the boxes and chests, taking more than sixty yuan in cash and various items of clothing and jewelry. They carried the stolen goods out of the house and scattered and fled. Afterwards, Chen's wife Lingyun reported to the Shiliupu Branch Bureau in charge, requesting them to pursue the robbers.

Traveler Commits Suicide by Poison 213

A traveler came to the Qinghe Inn in Qinghe Lane, Hubei Road, on the 12th of this month, claiming to be Zhang Minwei from Jiangsu, 40 years old, a merchant. The waiter led him to Room 123 on the upper floor, where he stayed for several days without any abnormalities. Until the night before, he secretly took raw opium and committed suicide. The waiter discovered him the next morning, but he had already died. The waiter reported to the accounting room, who reported to the Old Zha Police Station, which sent Patrol Officer No. 226 to rush over. The body was sent to the Renji Hospital Group for examination, awaiting the court's examination.

Shanghai National Goods Company Holds an Elegant Game of Golden Arrow Pitch-Pot 215

The Shanghai National Goods Company, located opposite the Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, prepares various national goods and studies sales methods every year. It is heard that today they are holding a "Golden Arrow Pitch-Pot" game. This game is one of the ancient palace games. The company uses it to arouse customers' elegance and has prepared nine kinds of grand prizes. Anyone who buys national goods worth more than two yuan can go upstairs to participate. Mr. Wang Pingnan has written a five-character poem for it: "Oblique Row Nine Grades Award, Guiding Arrow One Pitch-Pot, Standing Watch for High Skill, Together Support National Goods." As for the prizes, they are marked on the list. If a customer wants to obtain a certain prize, they can obtain it by pitching the golden arrow into the pot of that prize. If they do not hit the pot, there are also extra gifts. This game is truly unprecedented in Shanghai. Its elegant significance is truly interesting and attractive, without any suspicion of favoritism or bias. Yesterday afternoon, the arrangements were already in place. Those who heard of this and came to visit were truly in a situation of being overwhelmed on the mountain road. The pitch-pot area is located in the children's playground on the second floor.

Chinese and Foreign Goods Association Retains Chairman Cheng Yujie 217

Unanimous Resolution of the 13th Executive and Supervisory Committee Meeting

Mr. Cheng Yujie, Chairman of the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Goods Trade Association, previously submitted his resignation to the association due to fatigue. This was reported in previous newspapers. It was heard yesterday that the association specially convened the 13th Executive and Supervisory Committee meeting. Chairman Ba Lingyun presided over the meeting with due formality. Secretary Fu Keming reported on Chairman Cheng Yujie's original letter requesting to resign and other documents. The following important matters were then resolved: (1) The publication date for the fifth issue of the Chinese and Foreign Monthly Magazine was postponed by fifteen days. (2) Regarding Chairman Cheng's letter requesting resignation, it was unanimously agreed that Mr. Cheng has worked diligently for the association and made significant contributions. Therefore, they sincerely requested him to remain in his position. The association's reply to Mr. Cheng is excerpted below: "Dear Sir, We have just received your letter humbly resigning from the position of Chairman. Today happened to be the date of the 13th Executive and Supervisory Committee meeting, so your letter was brought up for discussion. It was unanimously agreed that you have served the association diligently and tirelessly and are respected by all members. Moreover, the future development of the association's affairs depends on your talent and planning. How can we allow you to retire so hastily? Therefore, it was resolved to sincerely request you to remain in your position. We hereby record this decision in a letter and respectfully request you to consider it and continue to shoulder the arduous task for the benefit of the association. This is our sincere hope."

A Costume Ball Is Coming 220

Co-organized by Saint Anna Dance Hall and Yunshang Clothing

The history of dance halls in Shanghai is nearly twenty years, but there has never been a costume ball. This is because organizing such an event is costly, and it is difficult to collect costume samples. Therefore, although there are many dance halls in Shanghai, costume balls have been difficult to realize. The owner of Saint Anna Dance Hall, realizing that a costume ball could increase the interest of dancers, consulted with the famous Yunshang Clothing Company in Shanghai. He received the approval of the company's owner. Many costume samples were ordered from famous European and American fashion designers, all of which are in the 1935 style, with more than 500 styles. Mr. Wang selected 70 styles from the 500 styles and ordered all the dancers in the dance hall to make them separately. The cost is about 2,000 yuan. This matter has been in preparation for nearly two months. More than half of the costumes have been made. Both parties are now preparing everything, and the event is expected to be held in early February. This is also a new atmosphere in the dance world in the new year. It is also heard that Yunshang is offering special discounts to dance enthusiasts and welcomes custom-made costumes of various styles at special prices.

City News 221

Fulu Garden Restaurant Offers New Year's Eve Dinner. As the end of the year approaches, families traditionally eat New Year's Eve dinner. The dishes cooked by those skilled in cooking are mostly familiar, which is a fact. Those who are not in the culinary industry have limited knowledge, so they cannot innovate. Those who are not skilled in cooking will waste good ingredients, which is a pity. Recently, Fulu Garden (located at the intersection of Niuzhuang Road and Laohe Road, next to Yousheng Travel Agency, phone number 95365) has been particularly prosperous in this seasonal business because the prices are fair, the quantity is large, and the quality is good. The six yuan, eight yuan, and ten yuan "banquets" are most suitable for New Year's Eve dinners at home. Just a phone call is enough to have them delivered on time. This saves the trouble of buying and cooking and allows one to taste different flavors. It is no wonder that those who order dishes are overwhelmed, and their business is booming, surpassing all others in the industry.

Chen Jingzhang's Private Opium Den Was Discovered, He Refused to Appear in Court, and a Rascal Impersonated Him 226

The Judge Saw Through the Impersonation in Court and Was Furious

If He Fails to Appear Next Time, an Arrest Warrant Will Be Issued

Recently, Detective Bao Tai of the New Zha Police Station received a tip that Chen Jingzhang (also known as Wan Xie), a runner for the Yongfeng Money Shop on Ningbo Road, is from Shangyu, Zhejiang. In addition to running the money shop, he secretly runs a large-scale opium den at No. 9 Xiangfu Lane, Kader Road, in the Public Concession, exclusively for the consumption of opium by wealthy merchants and financiers from the upper class. His business is thriving, and his customers are always full. Therefore, the police obtained a search warrant. On the morning of the day before yesterday, Detective Bao Tai led Chinese detectives and constables to the opium den. First, they guarded the front and back doors and rushed upstairs. At that time, because it was still early, most opium smokers had not yet arrived to indulge. Therefore, only Chen Jingzhang himself was lying on a couch, smoking opium. He was arrested on the spot by the detectives. In the rooms, they found seven opium lamps, more than ten opium pipes, six opium guns, and more than thirty taels of opium paste. There was also a jade opium gun worth a lot of money, which was presumably used to supply special smokers. With the evidence in hand, they were taken to the police station. After a brief interrogation, Chen only admitted that he smoked it himself and did not provide it to others. Later that afternoon, a lawyer posted bail and released Chen. Yesterday morning, the police filed a public lawsuit, and the case was brought to the First Special Court. Judge Wu Tingqi opened the Eighth Criminal Court for trial. The police lawyer presented the case. However, Chen Jingzhang, fearing punishment, did not appear in court and instead hired a rascal whose name is unknown to impersonate him and appear in court. Judge Wu saw through the impersonation in court and was furious. The police also filed a public lawsuit under Article 10 of the Anti-Opium Law. If Chen Jingzhang fails to appear in court next time, a warrant will be issued to arrest him and punish his illegal activities. Judge Wu then ordered that the hearing be postponed to next Tuesday (the 22nd).

Western Football League Zilin Cup East China and Youyou Tie 228

Result: 3-3

The Western Football League Zilin Cup match between East China B and Youyou B was held at 3 PM yesterday at the Shen Garden Stadium. The two sides were evenly matched, and a fierce battle was expected. More than a thousand spectators attended. The first-team players of the two teams also came to the stadium to cheer. As a result, each team scored three goals, and the game ended in a draw.

Zhi Bin Opens the Scoring 229

Referee He Chunhui blew the whistle, and the athletes from both sides began to compete. Youyou had the opportunity to kick off and immediately took the offensive, but failed to score. East China took the opportunity to counterattack and penetrated deep into Youyou's territory. Shanfu Zhibin shot at the goal quickly and accurately, and the ball went into the net, only ten minutes after the start of the game.

Ji Liang Adds the Finishing Touch 230

After losing a goal, Youyou worked hard to counterattack. The five forwards were like hungry tigers devouring eagles. East China's goal became a scene of chaos. Xi Qiaosheng and Mao Hongfa had many opportunities to shoot at the goal, but they all missed. East China rose again and made a comeback. Jia Jiliang received a pass from Xu Jingcheng and shot fiercely, hitting the target again. The first half ended here, with East China winning 2-0.

Hui Pei Pulls Back a Goal 231

The two sides each had a lemon, and they changed sides to fight again. After losing two goals, Youyou was determined and worked hard to recover. Hui Pei intercepted a ball, went in alone, and shot perfectly at the goal, the ball entering from the corner of the goal, making the score 2-1.

Hongfa Scores Again 232

After Youyou regained a goal, their offensive was even fiercer than before. East China's goal was in a precarious situation. Mao Hongfa received a pass from the center, dribbled slightly to the appropriate position, gritted his teeth, and shot with a bang, the ball entering from the right corner. At this time, the score was 2-2.

Wen Kui Penalizes Twelve Yards 233

At this time, the two sides were evenly matched, and the players were eager to win, so their actions were quite rough. A certain player from East China was penalized twelve yards for an illegal collision. Xu Wenkui took the penalty and scored, making the score 3-2, with Youyou taking the lead.

Bao Jun Equalizes the Score 234

After the defeat, East China shook its spirits and hoped to fight to the death. While the two sides were fighting fiercely, Bao Jun of East China took a fierce offensive, breaking through two lines of defense in a row, aimed at the enemy's goal, and shot with all his might, the ball entering in response, making the score 3-3, and the two sides were evenly matched.

Beiping Normal University Research Institute Studies Teaching Materials for Various Subjects in Teacher Training 250

Six Types of Survey Forms Created

Education Bureau Distributes to Municipal Elementary Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to all municipal elementary schools yesterday, stating: "Upon receiving a letter from the Research Institute of National Beiping Normal University, it is stated that the teaching materials for various educational subjects in normal schools have a significant impact on the overall education of elementary schools. Whether the Ministry-approved standards and commercially available textbooks are perfect is still a question. Our institute plans to use scientific methods to study these teaching materials, providing reference for teachers in normal schools. However, this type of research is difficult to complete without broad support. Respectfully, we admire your bureau's promotion of research. We hereby submit six types of survey forms, each in four hundred copies, totaling two thousand four hundred copies, hoping that you will distribute them to teachers in municipal elementary schools who have graduated from full normal schools (six types for each person), requiring them to be completed and submitted within a limited time (one week). Your bureau will then compile and submit them to the Education College of Normal University. Enclosed are the survey forms. In addition to distributing them, please promptly issue six types of survey forms, two copies of each, totaling twelve forms, to the principals of the schools, instructing them to quickly distribute the forms to teachers who have graduated from full normal schools for completion. If the number of graduates from full normal schools exceeds two, common opinions should be included. The forms must be returned to the bureau within seven days of receiving this order for compilation and forwarding. This matter concerns educational research and should not be delayed. This order includes six types of survey forms: Survey Form for Administrative Teaching Materials in Normal Schools and Elementary Schools, Survey Form for Teaching Methods Teaching Materials in Normal Schools and Elementary Schools, Survey Form for Research Teaching Materials in Normal Schools and Elementary Schools, Survey Form for Introduction to Education Teaching Materials in Normal Schools, Survey Form for Educational Psychology Teaching Materials, Survey Form for Educational Testing and Statistics Teaching Materials, etc."

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Perseverance and Success 266

— Li Lai

Little friends, don't you all want to achieve your desires, or want to be a big figure in the future? I can say definitively that "desire is the mother of success," as long as you have perseverance and the spirit of fearlessness to do it, you will be able to achieve it sooner or later. If you don't believe me, I can give you an example:

Once upon a time, the king of McDunn hid in a dilapidated thatched hut after failing. At this time, he was very regretful, and his heart of revenge gradually disappeared with it. Later, he suddenly saw a spider making a web on a horizontal and vertical beam. It spat silk six times and finally failed, but it did not regret it. It continued to work hard to spit silk towards the place it had chosen. On the seventh time, it succeeded. This kind of action, an action with perseverance, moved the king. At this time, the king regained his spirits and summoned a hundred warriors to resist the enemy country. Sure enough, in a few days, he recovered the lost territory.

Little friends, "everyone can become Yao and Shun," don't underestimate yourselves. You are the great men of the future, if you have the perseverance of never giving up. Move forward! Your motherland is asking you for help!

Newton's Childhood 267

— Xi Dan

The great British scientist - Mr. Newton, was very weak when he was young; his mother spent all her efforts to raise him, fearing that he would not be able to support himself. Unexpectedly, he later developed his genius, created a great cause, and was always praised and worshipped by people.

Newton studied at a public school at the age of twelve; however, he was unwilling to study hard and his grades were not good. Later, because his classmates bullied him, he felt very painful, and then he made up his mind to study hard.

He wanted to apply all his knowledge to practice. Knives, saws, axes, and hammers were his commonly used tools, and he practiced his skills very skillfully. Although he was young, he often wanted to use his skills to try them out.

On a road near his village, someone built a windmill. He carefully investigated it, and completely understood the layout of the project and the structure of the machine. In a short time, he built a windmill in the same way and built it on his roof, rotating there non-stop. The internal mechanisms of his windmill were simple and had no difference from the original.

Little friends, we must know that he was able to do amazing things later, not entirely relying on talent, but because he was able to make up his mind!

(Note 1) Investigation means observing and thinking.

Not Afraid of the Cold 268

— Rong Yu

The little hero is willing to endure hardships and is also willing to work hard without avoiding difficulties. However, this kind of courage also requires accumulated cultivation. How can a pampered young master with a fragile body have such perseverance!

In this cold weather, everyone knows not to be afraid of the cold, and everyone will say it, but how many people can actually do it? I saw the foreign little heroes in the concession, wearing short coats, exposing their knees, carrying their schoolbags, and jumping to school in the cold wind and snow. Looking back at our little heroes, some of the parents who love them too much have already told them to warm themselves by the fire in the house and not let them go to school. Ordinary children also wear as bulky as camels, dragging their heavy steps listlessly.

The great British naval hero Nelson is a famous figure in history. When he was a child, he was afraid of the cold and did not go because of the wind and snow. His father said, "It's up to you whether you go or not, but being timid is not the attitude that a real man should have." He listened to these words, and immediately dragged his brother to school.

Little friends, in this cold weather, not being afraid of the cold is the same as Nelson. Then the future achievements may not be inferior to Nelson!

Min'er's Winter Vacation Cold Relief Method 269

— Linghu Zhao

Time flies so fast. In a flash, it's the winter vacation again. Many little friends are going home with their schoolbags. It really seems like a group of birds out of a cage, jumping around lively.

Dear little friends, during this long vacation, you may forget the books you have read because there is no teacher to supervise you. Even your parents think it's a vacation and let you go. Then you are in great danger. I believe that when you go back to school for the exam, you will definitely fail and not be able to move up to the next grade. This is so terrible and shameful!

Then, do we just study hard? That's not right either. Let me introduce you to Min'er's winter vacation cold relief method!

(1) Get up at seven o'clock, write two sheets of large and small regular script, and do breathing exercises outside the door.

(2) Do arithmetic and draw pictures at nine o'clock, and kick shuttlecocks with my younger brother.

(3) Play the organ and sing songs with my older brother within one hour in the afternoon.

(4) Read Chinese, write new words, and recite at two o'clock in the afternoon.

(5) Play with classmates at four o'clock. (Or ask my brother to take me to the park.)

(6) After dinner, ask my father to tell stories, or guess riddles with my younger brother, and finally write a diary and go to sleep.

Little friends, you can also make your own schedule and put it into practice.

Dr. Li Gave Me a Plus Sign 272

How Do Animals Spend the Winter? 273

— He Gongchao

It's getting cold, and we don't see many insects and birds anymore. Where did they go? Little friends, have you thought about it?

Animals, like people, are also afraid of the cold, and they also have ways to spend the winter. Look at the first picture, although the mantis is dead, it has already laid its eggs on the branches in the autumn. The outside of the eggs is wrapped in a layer of gelatinous substance, called the ootheca. The many eggs inside will not die after winter, and little mantises will be born again next summer. Look at the second picture again, as soon as winter comes, ants (so are bees) no longer come out, and hide in their nests to spend the winter. Because they have accumulated a lot of food in peacetime, they will not starve to death in winter. Look at the third picture again, frogs, snakes, turtles, etc. sleep in the soil to spend the winter, which is called hibernation. They don't eat anything at this time, but they won't starve to death, because they have stored a lot of nourishing things in their bodies, and they are slowly digesting there. Look at the fourth picture again, birds and beasts add to their feathers in winter, and their bodies don't feel cold. We humans have to wear more clothes in winter, but birds and beasts will add clothes themselves. Look at the fifth picture again, most of the fish and shrimp in the water hide in the mud under the ice and no longer swim to the surface of the water to come into contact with the cold air on the ice. Look at the sixth picture again, swallows know in advance that winter is coming, and fly to the warm south in the autumn to spend the winter. At the same time, geese fly from the north to our place, because the north is much colder than here.

Little Common Sense

Omens Before Rain 274

— Jun Peng

Little friends! When you go to school, it suddenly rains on the way, and your head is wet, like a lost chicken. Do you think: How boring is this? Originally, we could just look at the barometer to see if the weather is clear, but do we all have one? I think: Not necessarily! Little friends! The phenomena before it rains are indeed worth discussing. However, before we look at the text below, what changes in the weather before it rains, and what are the different and special places from sunny days? This kind of enlightenment is called an omen.

1. Swallows and sparrows flying high are omens of sunny days, and vice versa for rain.

2. Seeing distant mountains as near is an omen of rain.

3. Hearing distant bell sounds clearly is an omen of rain.

4. Coal smoke not rising is an omen of rain.

5. An eastern rainbow at sunrise, and a western rainbow is an omen of rain.

6. Eastern sunrise with a purple sky is an omen of rain.

7. The call of the hylid is an omen of rain soon to begin.

8. Ants returning to their nests is an omen of prolonged rain.

9. Dew on rice is an omen of a sunny day, and vice versa for rain.

10. Damp ground with sweat is an omen of rain.

11. Steam whistles sounding clearly from afar are omens of rain.

12. A halo around the moon is an omen of rain.

Research on Pencils 275

— Bitter

Many people today who use pencils for writing have not researched them in detail, assuming they are made of lead, which is a big mistake. In fact, pencils are made of graphite.

Graphite is mined from the earth, so it is a mineral, black and light in texture.

The materials for pencils are graphite, clay, cedarwood, and rubber. The manufacturing process is as follows: graphite and clay are mixed into a slurry and put into a hydraulic press. The machine has a mold with many holes, the diameter of which is the same as the desired thickness of the pencil lead. The graphite and clay slurry is pressed through this mold, forming long strips of pencil lead. These are cut, dried by a stove, and then they can be used.

The hardness or softness of the pencil lead is not due to the graphite itself, but to the amount of clay in the composition. In addition, the wood that protects the pencil lead must be soft and not easily bent to be suitable for use.

Children, don't look down on this small pencil, thinking it is not worth studying. In fact, everything in this universe has value for research.

Light Bulbs Transformed into Fish Tanks 276

— Daosheng

Fish tanks can be made from broken light bulbs. The method is very simple: first, remove the black, hard material on the bulb with a sharp iron tool. This part of the work is not difficult. After the black, hard material is removed, you will see a layer of glass connected to a small glass rod inside the bulb. Carefully break that layer of glass with a sharp nail, and the small glass rod can be taken out. There will be nothing inside the bulb, and it will be connected to the outside world. After adding water, you can raise small goldfish.

There are two small nails on the head of the bulb, which are usually used to attach it to the light socket. Now they can be easily removed. The two small holes that remain can be threaded with a thin string to hang up this homemade small fish tank.

Strange Zoo 277

— Wen Yuyang

Equine Animals

(1) Hartebeest: Found in Africa, it is a vertebrate, ruminant, even-toed ungulate. Its mane and tail are very similar to a horse. The difference is that it has horns. In the past, some people said it was rare for a horse to grow horns. Now we know that there are horned horses. Do you children find this strange?

(2) Hippopotamus: Also a type of horse, but it does not ruminate. Its body is more than ten feet long, its eyes and ears are very small, its mouth is very wide, its legs are very short, and each leg has four claws with webs connecting them. It likes to live in the water and can swim, sleeping during the day and coming out at night to look for food.

(3) Llama: Found in South America, it is a ruminant, even-toed ungulate. Some people say it is the camel of the Americas. Its body is about the size of a donkey, and it can carry goods through dangerous mountain ridges.

(4) Zebra: Found in South Africa, it is a vertebrate, odd-toed ungulate. Its body is six or seven feet long, its legs are very thin, and its entire body is silvery white with black stripes. Its vision, smell, and hearing are very sensitive, and it runs very fast, making it difficult to catch. Its appearance is also similar to a donkey, so it is also called a striped donkey. Have you children ever seen one in a movie?

The Adventures of Sinbad the Sailor (Part 3) 278

— Xinqing

As I was telling my story, several people came up on the ship. As soon as they saw me, they knew that I was Sinbad, who had often been on the same ship with them; so I didn't need to spend much time proving to the captain that I was not an imposter. Finally, he said, "Thank God, you are safe. Here are your goods; take them and do as you please."

When those packages were returned to my hands, I deeply thanked this person.

I said to him, "Please take some of my goods as a gift, because you are a righteous man!" But he said that he had no such intention.

So I gave the best of my goods to King Melechi, because he had treated me so kindly. He was very happy to hear of my good fortune.

Before long, I boarded the ship that carried my packages and returned to my hometown.

The people in my house were happy to see me, because I had been gone for a long time and they all thought I was dead. I built a magnificent house, bought slaves and land, because I had decided to spend the rest of my years in Baghdad.

Sinbad's Second Voyage

Soon I wanted to change my life. I volunteered to do business again, so I bought goods and transported them to sea in preparation for the next trip. We traveled to various places, and my goods sold very well.

One day we came to an island covered with various fruit trees. We went ashore, but wherever we went, we could not see any traces of people or animals.

I left my friends and sat down by a stream, eating a hearty meal of the food I had brought. Then I lay down, and soon I fell fast asleep.

Commercial News

Major Financial Players Watch as Gold Market Falls 2.1 Yuan 279

The gold market is quiet, lacking change, and major players are watching, resulting in only 1.9 jiao fluctuations in half a day. This is a typical phenomenon for the end of the lunar year. Since the morning, overseas silver markets saw the British pound rise and the US dollar remain flat. Deferred silver prices in Monterrey decreased, exchange rates remained steady, and spot gold in London rose by 2.5 pence. Off-site preliminary trading initially reached 71.2 yuan, but due to rumors of US purchases after the close of large transactions, most speculative long positions immediately adopted a selling strategy. Major players provided a slight supply, and at one point supply exceeded demand, causing a sharp decline and retreating to within 70 yuan. Low opening prices were heard in the morning, slightly weak. Subsequently, the official announcement of the central bank's listing, with both British pound and US dollar flat and customs gold units rising by 0.3%, and the benchmark gold price at 993.1 yuan, stimulated speculative buying. Major players seized the opportunity to buy at low prices, causing a rebound. However, the major barrier of 70 yuan was never breached, and the banks' appetite seemed full. Buyers returned to activity, and prices fell after rising. However, due to the banks' short-covering, many buyers also bought at low prices, causing a rebound. It was learned that the Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's listing showed the British pound up 1.25 and the US dollar up 0.25. The banks still had a selling appetite. At this time, prices hovered around 9 yuan. Later, as more positions were released, the number of sellers increased temporarily, leading to weakness. However, major players bought aggressively at low prices, allowing prices to be maintained. The announcement of the silver equalization tax remained unchanged, still at 6%. Calculated at 1 shilling and 5 pence and 71875, although there was no stimulus, prices subsequently rebounded. The banks' appetite went from full to short-covering. Market prices rose from low to high, but because major players were supplying at the 70 yuan level, it was difficult to break through, and the rising trend was hindered. Supply became abundant, and prices fell back. Trading was limited. Thereafter, supply and demand balanced, and prices hovered between 9.1 jiao and 9.5 jiao, making the situation extremely boring. The overall trend was dull until the noon close. The market situation was mediocre in the first half of the day, making it extremely difficult to stir up any waves. This was because there was a lack of stimulus for prices to rise, and there were concerns about the central bank releasing cash after prices fell, which contributed to the situation. The swap spread was still around 7 yuan. The market situation for the first half of the day is recorded below.

The opening price in the morning was 969.9 yuan, down 1.7 yuan from the previous close. Hengchangyong first sold and retreated to 8.8 yuan. The central bank's listing was announced, and customs gold rose by 0.3%. Yongli, Hengyu, Yuanchangyong, and others increased positions, rising to 70 yuan. Mitsui sold US dollars for February at 0.5 yuan, and speculative investors, as well as Changda, Hengxingyuan, Chenyu, and Hengyu sold, retreating to 68.2 jiao. However, the importers were unwilling to lower prices, so futures were not sold. Spot foreign rice was still handled smoothly by local and inland merchants. There seemed to be a rising trend in the morning. In the afternoon, 20,000 bags arrived from Saigon and another 4,000 bags were transferred from Hong Kong. The importers' appetites turned sluggish, and the market also held steady. The total daily trading volume was 3,500 bags of Saigon rice and 1,700 bags of rice. Recently, there has been a slight arrival of customer rice, and the sales have also been active. The market is in a stable situation. More than 3,000 bags were opened yesterday and were still handled by local and inland merchants in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The market price did not move.

The River Down Rice Market Turned Weak 296

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources for various merchants were scarce again, with only over 30 ships arriving (a total of 5-6,000 shi). The retail market and the mill's appetites were also sluggish, so the market was particularly flat. Fortunately, the arrivals were scarce, and the arrivals and sales were balanced, so the market could still be stable. However, the environment was poor, and morale was relatively low. Although the prices of various grades of thick japonica rice and late rice did not fluctuate much, the situation was inevitably soft. The market for varieties such as Dujian and Yinbian Yuan was also weak because the sales channels turned sluggish.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, more than 20 ships arrived from various routes down the river. The market's appetite for various colors of glutinous rice was still weak. Bian Yuan was slightly traded, and the prices of thin rice and early rice were slightly reduced. The remaining goods were sluggish. The market price of white glutinous rice was also stable. The middle and lower grades were slightly weaker. Bian Yuan fell in price by 1-2 jiao. The remaining goods, except for the continued slight decline in thin rice, showed a downward trend.

Foreign Sesame Rose Another 3 Jiao 297

—Yellow Bean Factory Demand Still Strong—

Yesterday, the appetite for foreign sesame was still strong. A total of 1,400 tons were traded in the market, with delivery scheduled for January and February. Most of it was handled by Yige, and the rest was handled by Sassoon. The market price rose another 3 jiao, opening at 10.05 yuan. The overall trend was still strong. Spot trading was extremely lively. A total of 1,6-700 bags of various sesame varieties were traded in the market. The market price increased by 6-7 fen. The situation followed the strong trend of foreign merchants' net goods.

Recently, several factories had strong demand for yellow beans, so the price continued to rise by 8-9 fen. It was estimated that there were about 18-9 vehicles of Dalian beans, 800 silk bags of Hankou vehicle beans, over 3,000 bags of Gui beans, 2 vehicles of Yingzhou beans, 2 vehicles of Bengbu beans, 300 bags of Tancheng beans, over 300 bags of Shashi beans, 2,500 bags of Hankou beans, 580 bags of Hankou late beans, and 1 vehicle of Niuzhuang white flat beans. Most of the sales were to oil mills, and the rest were for export and to local inland areas.

Sugar Market Chaoqing Sugar and Foreign Plates Slightly Decreased 298

Yesterday's sugar market trend was flat. Due to Saturday, there was not much trading. Moreover, the Lunar New Year is approaching, and sales after that may be difficult to be smooth. The association's plate for 24 coarse sand white and spot goods was 18.73 yuan, which was 3 fen better than before. Dutch red was quoted at the original price but not traded. Taikoo sugar B mark was 19.15 yuan, down 5 fen from the previous day. The local factory's first-grade fine white sugar was 18 yuan. The current goods that could be delivered from Chaoqing were 10.8 yuan, followed by 10.45 yuan to 9.8 yuan. The middle and lower grades were 1-2 jiao lower than before.

North-South Goods Haikou Branches Opened 2,600 Boxes 299

Decreased by 5 Jiao

Haikou branches had not been opened for a long time due to the poor market. However, the total number of goods arriving before and after was less than 3,000 boxes. Now that the end of the total settlement period was approaching, there was no hope of rising prices. Therefore, after both the merchants and the dealers contacted each other, their opinions gradually converged. In the past two days, after evaluating the various goods, they decided to open all of the remaining 2,600 boxes, which was 5 jiao lower than the previous plate. The distribution was handled by various firms.

Oil Market 300

Asphalt Arrivals Scarce, Market Tight

The arrival of asphalt from various places was scarce, especially from Hankou. This was because after strict management by Zao, there was even more shortage of spot goods in the Hankou market. It was also heard that dealers still had a certain amount of orders, so even with a small number of arrivals, dealers and agents competed for them, resulting in a tight market. Heavy Jing oil had already reached over 12 liang, and those with wood also required 12 liang. As such, it was undeniable that there were not many arrivals in the Hankou market before the final settlement, and the inventory was low. Local dealers in this port also did not have any accumulation. Fortunately, the sales market this winter was not as strong as in previous years, so it was barely able to cope. If it had been as strong as in previous years, the shortage would have been even more severe. Due to only 30% harvest this year, the local vehicle oil from Jiaxing in western Zhejiang has not yet arrived in Shanghai. According to the current market price, it costs 22 yuan per dan to deliver to Shanghai, which is more than 2 yuan higher than Hankou Jing oil. Although the quality is said to be better, the price feels too high and seems not cost-effective. However, there are occasional candle makers who need it and must use it, so they purchase a small amount to add some embellishment.

Metal Bamboo Steel Bars' Arrivals and Sales Are Smooth 301

—White Lead Skin Market Still Sluggish—

Although the new arrivals of bamboo steel bars are smooth, the sales are also strong, so the market is very lively. The prices for various styles are between 170 yuan and 120 yuan. Among the trading merchants, those from Fuzhou, Hankou, and Qingdao are the most active. Among the local businesses, the construction industry is the most enthusiastic. It was found that a total of 3-400 tons have been traded in the past few days. It was heard that over 100 tons of next year's goods have also been thrown out, and the price is 1-2 yuan better than the current market.

Although industry peers are working hard to promote white lead skin these days, there is still little development due to the approaching settlement period and tight credit. Although the foreign price is rising, there is still no possibility of improvement. Therefore, the best-selling style is estimated at 26.5 yuan per dan, the ordinary style is estimated at 25 yuan, and the best fruit tea color is still quoted at around 24 yuan. It is heard that when the tea merchants and printing houses start business next year, the market price may increase.
