Women's World

Ms. Hua Luoshen Speaks on Chinese Women's Issues 321

— Xie Qing

According to the "Shishi Xinbao" of the 13th of this month, the Beiping Women's Federation recently invited Madam Hua Nan Gui, former Director of the Beiping Municipal Bureau, to give a lecture. It is said that she is of French nationality, proficient in literature, and has written famous works such as the film script "Love and Sacrifice" and "Wen Xing," which were adopted by Lianhua Film Company.

The topic of the lecture was "Chinese Women's Issues." According to her, Chinese women have three problematic areas: (1) Chinese women do not pay attention to hygiene, (2) they have bad habits, and (3) they do not like to read books and newspapers.

This is what is called a problem!

This is indeed a problem, but generally speaking, isn't this the issue facing the majority of Chinese women? This is just a problem for the wealthy women and ladies of China. They eat well, dress well, and do not need to work. If they do not learn some bad habits such as playing mahjong, smoking opium, drinking alcohol, etc., how do you expect them to live? Smoking opium and drinking alcohol are naturally unhygienic, but what use is reading books and newspapers to them? - Maybe they will read newspapers, but what they mainly read is probably about dog racing, horse racing events, and sensational, erotic movie advertisements, which have nothing to do with Chinese society or the liberation of Chinese women.

If the problem is understood in this way by Ms. Hua Luoshen, then the solution to the problem is naturally limited. It is said that she suggested "creating a type of small ticket, similar to a postage stamp, and affixing it to envelopes, sending them everywhere, so that people will see it and be alerted..."

This is the solution to women's issues! If this can really "alert" those degenerate women and make them realize something, that would indeed save a lot of effort. However, I think the problem will have to be prolonged. Even if they want to change this kind of life, how will they live their lives in the future! - History has destined them to be upper-class women who do not need to work.

The issue of Chinese women cannot be grasped on such superficial phenomena by a woman who is "proficient in literature." The women's issue is originally just a link in the entire social issue. To trace the root of its occurrence, it is necessary to investigate the social system that forms the women's issue.

The tragic situation of Chinese women, I think, cannot be seen by the eyes of a public official's wife. Almost no one needs to "alert" them. Life experiences will show them: they feel pain, they feel uncomfortable!

Indeed, the majority of Chinese women are unhygienic: their living conditions do not allow them to be "hygienic" at all. Chinese women have to start working for more than ten hours a day before they are fully developed. Chinese female workers are not allowed to take leave to rest during pregnancy by factory owners. Unemployed women in China, women trafficked from rural areas, they are forced to work as prostitutes, and thus, to meet the needs of the upper class, they become accustomed to some bad habits... Are all of these their wishes? Are they their own sins?

The majority of Chinese women grow up under the educational principle of the feudal consciousness that "a woman's lack of talent is a virtue," or they are rejected by capitalistic commercial schools, making most of them illiterate. Talking to them about reading books and newspapers is clearly putting the cart before the horse, isn't it?

The Intellectual Women of Hengyang 322

— Hua

Hengyang is a county town on the bank of the Xiang River in Hunan.

Culturally, it is not a very backward place. On the contrary, it is very dynamic because it is a transportation hub that tightly controls the upstream cities of the Xiang River, second only to Changsha, the provincial capital. The people are rich in barbaric temperament, and often fight and shed blood over trivial matters. - Women growing up in such an environment, in schools, often launch struggles to expel incompetent teachers because of their own interests; in society, there are also rare cases of sacrificing for the revolution. But all of these now seem to have become relics of the past, and like the civil rights movement to win female seats in the county council at that time, they have faded away lonely. Intellectual women have become more vulgar and more corrupt. The blood of revolutionary women has not inspired their self-awareness, self-confidence, and glorious memory, but what revolves around their lamb-like minds is: "That kind of sacrifice is terrible, we should protect ourselves wisely; what does it mean? Life is only a hundred years!" Due to the disillusionment given to them by democratic slogans, they are at a loss and can only drill deeper into the "selfish" corner, wasting that pitiful, cowardly life. However, the economic panic of the times does not allow them to live a life of "non-contention with things." They fight each other openly and secretly to seize the positions in a few small schools. Therefore, the interest struggles of female students are often confused and used as a tool for the struggle for someone's private position. In various government agencies, there are not one or two women as decorations. As for women's organizations, not to mention, they are completely zero.

In this way, women who have left their hometowns and obtained higher education diplomas, without the backing of wealthy gentlemen or even tougher backstage supporters, can't even think of entering the educational circles of Hengyang. And these few highly educated women are really too unfortunate - university diplomas and lovers are the purpose and meaning of their pursuit of knowledge, and they are the destination of their lives. They sit leisurely at home every day. The elegant ones blow and sing, chant and recite; the vulgar ones play cards, and mahjong; they can't talk about being a "good wife and loving mother," but the university diploma is like a golden signboard, enough for them to despise everything and live as parasites.

Almost universally, the consciousness of intellectual women in Hengyang is feudal. They have no deeper understanding of their own problems, nor do they have conscious actions. Not to mention a group that flatter their in-laws and hateful husbands, even women who have snatched marital autonomy from their parents often cry with swollen eyes behind people's backs, but do not have the courage to jump out of the established trap. There are even young widowed teachers who are neither for "love" nor for "singlehood." They shamelessly tell in the crowd, with a burst of praise following the sigh, the funny scene unfolds, like a "puppet show" being performed. - Naturally, the manipulators of this "puppet show" are not wandering performers, but man-eating "rites." "Fatalism" dominates them. Whether middle-aged women or young girls, after a violent and embarrassing entanglement of all their own sorrows, they helplessly lower their heads: "It's destined, there is no possibility of improvement!"

Therefore, many who were lively students or teachers ten years ago now have nothing but beds and stoves; they live in a state of depression, living like in a dream, unwilling to be seen by an old classmate, hiding as if they were dead, completely forgotten by society.

And the group that is active in society has never heard of a page of glorious life. Feudal threats, "fatalism" are their salvation. It can be said that after searching the entire city of Hengyang at this moment, there will not be such a woman who yearns for political suffering. In their scope of activity - schools - there is full of stagnation and lifeless depression. Pitiable are some of the students attending classes, sitting in the classroom, they are simply puppets, either listening quietly for an hour, or copying from the blackboard for an hour; there is no automatic questioning; when answering the teacher's words, the voice is timid and trembling, strangely dull. The auditorium is hung with students' compositions, drawings, and handicrafts, etc., but apart from stereotyped imitation, there are few, or even none, creative expressions. If there is a proposal for educational reform, this nosy outsider will be ridiculed: they do not avoid the frontal attack, but laugh it off, or answer: "It won't work, teacher! This place is destroyed as soon as it encounters something new, do you still want to eat? Everyone is the same, so-so. We are satisfied if we can inject some inherent knowledge into the students." This "get by" doctrine is the outlook on life and the spirit of career for intellectual women in Hengyang.

But their treatment is unusually pitiable! The principal of a county elementary school, working all day in a school where students have no autonomy, receives a salary of only a little more than twenty yuan; teachers are paid by the hour, with thirty or so hours per week, and piles and piles of papers are stacked on the desk, which they have to read until late at night, but they only earn around forty yuan. - However, this is a considerable amount! There are many who earn several yuan, or a dozen yuan.

It is simply unimaginable how they are saving in their lives; some people are still able to have surplus and buy real estate. What kind of decadent tendency is shining in their soul that is calculating painstakingly! …

Speaking of their entertainment, that is, pastime, few are willing to take books as their object - naturally, they have little time is also a reason. What is boring is that they learn the old tricks of licentious poets playing with women, "powdered chrysanthemum," "golden rouge," relish them with relish, fascinated, and hang them on their lips. When the daily four-page newspaper comes, they first compete to read this kind of news, and recite those frivolous poems praising the actors; when they are in the mood, they go to the theater together. In addition, there are occasional card games. Secular gifts and banquets, without exception, no matter how difficult life is, they can struggle to get up; "decency" is very important to them.

Vulgar, corrupt - intellectual women of Hengyang! I can't write in more detail; sympathy blocks my heart, and my pen is stiff. Recalling, the joys of childhood, the unforgettable or more or less affectionate friendships, here, friends, in a higher sense, hoping that you, who are far away from the mountains, regard this lightly sketched thing as a more advanced expression of love, a hint in a dream. I wish you a brave survival! May we have a more powerful reunion!

Eradicating Women's Jealousy 323

— Yun Ni

If we acknowledge that psychological phenomena are a reflection of social phenomena, then women's jealousy is certainly created by a certain social environment. Jealousy is not only found in women, but also in men, but women express it more intensely. Needless to say, jealousy is the most unpromising and despicable psychology. This is because this psychology is almost purely based on selfish individualism, and often circles in the narrowest range or dead end, and even leads to the most base and cruel actions. However, in the final analysis, jealousy is still a product of the current social system, a concrete manifestation of the most acute and deteriorated private ownership concept. Therefore, in the current society, anything that I do not have, or that others have better than me, can arouse jealousy. "Colleagues are jealous of each other" in industry and commerce is well known. Even if people have knowledge, ability, talent, or even are born beautiful, or invent scientific and mechanical inventions, they can attract the attention of jealousy. The heavier the selfishness, the shallower the knowledge, the narrower the mind (the narrowness and breadth of the mind is partly inherited), the more intense the jealousy - this can almost become a law. Conversely, people who can see through the structure of the private ownership system, understand the relationships within it and its inevitable causal laws, have far-sighted vision and the ambition to transform society, and are determined to sacrifice themselves and strive for the common happiness of mankind, will have their jealousy reduced to the weakest position, or even completely washed away.

The reason why women are particularly rich in jealousy is due to women's particular history and particular social environment, and family environment. Historically, women have been thrown into a realm of multiple oppression and humiliation, and often confined to the narrowest family circle, first of all, they have cultivated a very narrow psychology, and secondly, the accumulation of various inequalities and dissatisfactions, coupled with the abundance of emotions and the lack of reason... These, combined with the concept of private ownership and flourishing, have formed a particularly active and rampant nest of jealousy. Therefore, women not only see others being more dramatic and powerful than themselves and become jealous, see others having more clothes and jewelry and become jealous, see other women being more beautiful and smart than themselves and become jealous, even the elder sister-in-law sees the second sister-in-law giving birth to a good-looking or smart child and becomes jealous. The most wonderful thing is: such as a widowed mother, seeing her son being good with his daughter-in-law and becomes jealous... In the extreme of jealousy, even the elder sister-in-law kills or maims the second sister-in-law's child, and the mother torments or kills the daughter-in-law, all kinds of cruel and base behaviors are not uncommon. Nowadays, women who have received so-called new-style education certainly have much less jealousy, but generally speaking, traditional habits are still very deep. This is enough to prove it only from the disharmony among female colleagues in agencies, schools... the mutual competition for leadership positions in groups, or the various facts of slandering each other behind their backs, but they are expressed more elegantly and smartly in form, or they are not visible. Naturally, there are also women who have escaped from that narrow and despicable jealousy because of the firm will to transform society and the heroic spirit of self-sacrifice. However, this is ultimately a minority. Since women's jealousy and people's general jealousy belong to one of the psychological phenomena, are the degradation of the concept of private ownership, and are reflections of social phenomena, then we cannot simply curse this evil root of humanity like moralists or religious figures! Jealousy, but we should understand that this "evil root" is only the inevitable result reflected under this certain social system. To eradicate this "evil root," we must of course start from fundamentally transforming society. However, from an individual point of view, especially from a woman's point of view, we should also subjectively learn the despicableness of jealousy, and we should recognize that jealousy is the demon that destroys our female unity, and is a major obstacle in the course of the women's liberation movement. We must eradicate it from the root.

Quan Jie Tang 324

— Zhuang Qidong

— One of the Travelogue to Songjiang —

One door after another door, tightly locking the young woman's youth, this feudal ancient palace, Quan Jie Tang!

When we walked to the last two major doors, everyone felt gloomy and lifeless. Each major door was added with a large lock, and in addition to the large lock, a guard was added.

Because it was New Year's Day, there were especially many children in Quan Jie Tang. These children were raised by the widows in the past. Now, some are studying in school and come back at night, and some are playing there all day long. Their board and lodging are borne by the Quan Jie Tang, and the boys must leave there when they reach the age of thirteen.

The air in the courtyard is very silent. Not to mention that it seems to them that there is no change, even to us, these few desolate small trees seem to be surviving forever without seasons, surviving!

Opposite the courtyard are rows of rural-style houses, one floor and one bottom, which are the bedrooms of the widows, the detention centers of sex. The upstairs and downstairs are the same size, about two zhang wide and long. It is said that two families live in each room.

A woman of sixteen or seventeen years old was sitting by the upstairs window, observing. No, to be more precise, she was gazing, gazing at this group of uninvited travelers, gazing at the changing clouds in the sky. She seemed to be thinking about something, half-covering the wooden window, shaking her head lightly in disappointment. She was recalling, or she was thinking about her future destiny!

"How many people are there here?" I asked an old woman near me. She was forty or fifty years old. She was sewing a man's long trousers stitch by stitch. She stopped her needle and answered timidly:

"A lot!"

"Can people of all ages come in?"

"No, no, people over thirty cannot enter the hall!"

"Then what about you?"

"Me," she laughed, "I entered the hall when I was young. Which of these old women didn't enter the hall when they were young!"

With that, she continued to sew the clothes. Her face suddenly became gloomy, probably because she felt the difficulty and uselessness of the process from being a young widow to being an old widow.

After a moment of silence, I greedily asked her again:

"How many meals do you eat here a day?"

"Three meals."

"How many bowls of vegetables?"

"Two people only have one bowl of vegetables."

"Is it meat or vegetarian?"

"Usually it's vegetarian. There are two big meat meals and four small meat meals every ten days. But there are also extra dishes for festivals."

"Can you go back?"

"No, we can only go back once during the Qingming Festival to sweep the tombs."

"Who takes care of your clothes and the children's clothes?"

"It's all our own."

"Where do you get the money?"

"Some is sent from home, and some is earned by doing work."

"Is the pay for doing work big?"

"How can it be big, it's always several times less than usual."

Because we were going to visit other places again, I asked her the last question:

"What is your hope in life?"

"In the children!"

She answered in a startled and hesitant way. But soon, she seemed to deny herself, shaking her head in frustration. She stopped talking.

On the way back, our companions were all satisfied, occasionally talking about: "It's a pity that time is too hasty, we can't visit in more detail."

"We are very lucky to be able to see this secret of mankind."

"This is a mirror, reflecting the fate of women, reflecting how a woman's life ends up!"

The Tragedy of Xing Meimei 325

— Lian Rui

A few days ago, I received a letter from my sister, knowing that Xing Meimei, from the family of my uncle, has gone to her husband's house to guard the door as a widow. The Zhang family is wealthy, and Xing Meimei's living expenses are naturally not a problem, but it is very pitiful to be a widow at the age of seventeen. Moreover, since her mother-in-law wanted to retain the right to manage the family property, she would have persuaded my aunt to trick Xing Meimei into performing the tragedy of marrying a spirit tablet in the past, how can it be guaranteed that it was not her mother-in-law who persuaded her to say that "she is willing to remain a widow for life" now? How can a lively girl fall in love by looking at a fiancé lying on a coffin board, and be willing to remain a widow for him? Xing Meimei is very naive. At such a young age, she must not know how to use any tricks. It must be her mother-in-law's sweet words that moved her heart, so she said it was her own will, right?

"My aunt is really confused, and she is still hoping that the President will award her a chaste widow's memorial tablet. She is ruining her daughter's lifelong happiness in exchange for a chaste widow's memorial tablet?" This is the conclusion in my sister's letter. After reading the letter, I was stunned for five or six days. Xing Meimei graduated from junior high school last summer vacation. Could it be that even this bit of life knowledge was not given to her by the so-called school education? I can hardly believe this is true.

More than ten years ago, before the May Fourth Movement, my alma mater also had such an incident. The classmate who was tricked was the most beautiful girl in the whole school. Because there was no custom of electing school flowers or school queens at that time, everyone just secretly envied her in their hearts and did not give her any glorious titles. The main culprit who tricked her was her elder sister, because she wanted to adopt her son to her so as to obtain that rich inheritance. As a result, several years later, the virgin who originally wanted to be a chaste widow, because she could not bear the loneliness of widowhood, changed into a concubine of a certain warlord. The stubborn father actually published a notice in the newspaper to sever his relationship with her as a father and daughter. But that was after all more than ten years ago, how can I believe that there will be a victim of "waiting for a spirit at the door" more than ten years later? But although I don't believe it, the fact is still a fact! This makes me deeply suspicious of the current women's education.

"Second cousin Ai Jian, last year I escaped to Hangzhou to work because I didn't want to marry a consumptive ghost. In September, I was expelled for going on strike with others. After returning home, my father said that his consumption had been cured and asked me to go over. I believed it was true. My brother and sister-in-law wouldn't let me eat. I got married, worshipped heaven and earth, and was sent into the bridal chamber. I learned that he didn't even have the strength to worship the hall, so I cried and refused to share a bed. My mother-in-law said good things and begged me to do good deeds and leave a piece of flesh and blood for her son, a lifeline. I don't want to harm myself. I sleep in the same bed with the young maid every night. My father is ruthless and cannot discuss it with him. My brother came back for the New Year. I borrowed a few dollars from him and wanted to escape to Shanghai to work. I am willing to do any kind of rough work, it is better to be a widow. Please ask my aunt for me, I am afraid that her factory needs odd jobs. I want to be a widow and not do it. It is better to make my own living and be happy. Do you think it's right, I wish you

Happiness. Cousin Ai Lian's hand"

I read Lianmei's letter to me a year ago again and again, and the more I read it, the more suspicious I became. Why is it that a cousin who has only read for three and a half years in elementary school is more knowledgeable than a cousin who graduated from junior high school? Is it getting more and more confused the more you read?

I think, if it is not because of different school education, it must be because my second uncle, Lianmei's father, is a farmer, and my uncle is a teacher, and has taught Xing Meimei to read more ancient books since she was a child. Poor Xing Meimei, I don't know when she will be able to learn and understand? Whenever I think of her tragic marriage to a spirit tablet, my heart contracts so tightly that it is as uncomfortable as if I can't breathe.

Women and Literature 326

— Qian Zijin

(1) Women Reflected in Ancient Literature

(2) Ibsen, the Discoverer of the Female Soul

(3) Women After Ibsen

(4) Women of the Future

(1)

Literature is a mirror reflecting social life and a signal calling for the improvement of human life. Writers use their ingenious pens to reflect social life and expose all aspects of society. At the same time, they suggest new problems that the public has not yet recognized, drawing people's attention and understanding.

Throughout history, the lives of half of humanity, women, have left traces that we can find in literature. We can search literature for the discovery of female personality and soul, and the fresh accounts of women awakening and rising to improve their lives. From the image of women reflected in literature, we can clearly see the journey women have taken over thousands of years.

The women depicted in ancient literature are all pathetic creatures without independent personalities or souls. They are either playthings or slaves. The Yuefu "Midnight Song" says:

"Her wrist extends upon her lover's knee, what place is not pitiable?" This explains that the purpose of women is simply to make men feel "pitiable."

Consider another ancient poem:

"I go up the mountain to gather weeds, and down the mountain, I meet my former husband; I kneel and ask my former husband, how is the new bride?" It tells of a woman who was abandoned by her husband and suffered much pain. Later, she went up the mountain to gather wild vegetables, and on her way back, she encountered that heartless husband. She even knelt down and asked her husband, "Is the new bride well?" The husband replied, "The new bride is not as beautiful as you, nor as fast at weaving."

From this poem, we can see that the abandoned woman not only does not dare to resent, but when she meets her husband, she kneels down and asks about the new bride. This is simply not treating herself as a human being. The husband's reply only says that she is not as beautiful or as fast at weaving. Isn't this clearly treating women as slaves?

Cui Yingying in "Romance of the West Chamber" is also simply a complete plaything. She is dedicated from head to toe, from body to soul, to the lustful Zhang Sheng.

Although Lin Daiyu in "Dream of the Red Chamber" is written as very clever and self-respecting, she makes people feel pity for her everywhere. So melancholic and painful, so frail, she can be said to be the representative and typical of old-fashioned women. She lacks any independent spirit. Once she loses the protection or play of men, she cannot survive.

We can also see the same soulless and independently-personality women of the old era in Western literature. In the novels of Turgenev and Chekhov, we can recognize many charming and sensual women. From the novels of Zola and Maupassant, we can see many gentle and obedient slaves. In Tolstoy's novels, there is Anna Karenina, who is a slave to fate. In Thomas Hardy's novels, we can see Tess, who can never escape the clutches of a villain.

Women of the past, as the Bible says, "are a rib from man," attached to men, without soul or personality. It can be seen that whether in China or abroad, women in savage times were equally unfortunate, equally serving as slaves or playthings of another kind of people. They carefully flattered their masters, serving them diligently. Or they deliberately feigned coyness and obedience, without anyone's pity. The husbands, however, did whatever they wanted and acted tyrannically for a while. Or they used some clever skills and sweet names to anesthetize women, causing them to fall without realizing it. Thus, women lived their lives in a dark and sunless underground.

(2)

Women are not born slaves or playthings. They originally had beautiful souls and independent personalities. However, they were submerged by long-term oppression and traditional thoughts and habits, intoxicated by ingenious tricks and skills, and the occasional depression was flattened in their own bitter cries. So they became soulless animals. This inhuman life of theirs went through a long period until the great writer Ibsen was born.

Ibsen's problem play "A Doll's House," everyone knows, is a wake-up call for women, a signal to awaken women. It awakened women from their millennia-long dreams, and fully exposed the cold, tyrannical exterior and interior of men. He uncovered the hypocrisy of all the sins and deceptions that men have always asked of them, allowing women to recognize them. Thus, the soul of women, which had never been noticed and which women themselves had forgotten, was suddenly discovered and awakened by this great writer. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement Amateur Weekly

Amateur Musings

What Books Should Young People Read? 327

— Zhuang Mingyi

The purpose of reading is to gain knowledge. Books are a tool, and people must be able to use and control them to get the most out of them. For example, a carpenter must choose sharp chisels, axes, etc., to help him with his work. It is essential to carefully select books to read.

Some time ago, Mr. Liang Qichao published his "Must-Read List of Books for National Studies." In October of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, the "Dawan Bao" newspaper sought "Books I Would Like to Introduce to Young People," and many people responded. Mr. Shi Zhicun recommended the books "Zhuangzi" and "Selections of Refined Literature" to young people. This caused a heated debate.

Therefore, it is not easy to make a definitive statement about the answer to "What Books Should Young People Read?" I think that rather than listing a bunch of wild book titles, it would be better for everyone to study and come up with several "principles for selecting books to read," so that ambitious young people can find suitable books based on these principles.

Based on our daily life, the books we should read can be roughly divided into three aspects: (1) those related to personal cultivation, (2) those related to professional knowledge, and (3) those related to leisure education.

Young people are in a period of personal transformation, and it is necessary to cultivate personal life and career at any time. Although we do not need to worship idols, we can seek from the famous people of the past the special qualities that made them famous. Reading books on cultivation can give us an opportunity for reflection and be the basis for changing our temperament.

The knowledge gained in school is mostly general education knowledge. Although university courses have more specialized research, in reality, because they are not yet related to real business, the knowledge gained may not be useful for business. A person who leaves school will feel his lack of knowledge. Many practical knowledge feels insufficient. Why is this? Originally, the knowledge gained before was empty. Now, when it comes into contact with real life, it is discovered that what was learned emptily before may not be practical or may not have been noticed at the time. Therefore, to seek the improvement of business, it is necessary to obtain knowledge related to business.

Books for appreciation should not be discarded either. It is like eating rice and definitely needing to drink water. People's lives must not only be a monotonous life of material and numbers but also a happy and beautiful life of the spirit. Literature and art can make up for the shortcomings of life. They express a more genuine life, which is enough to enable us to understand a more meaningful life. Although literature and art cannot make material contributions and inventions like science, they have fulfilled the responsibility of cultivating people's emotions and comforting people's souls. Therefore, when you have spare time every day after work, appreciating these kinds of books is the best form of leisure education.

Zhuangzi said: "My life has a limit, but knowledge has no limit." Since we cannot completely consume the limited time of our lives in the endless pile of books, then how can we not find the books we need from the vast sea of books?

Hobbes once said to people: "If I also read as many books as others, I am afraid I will also be as ignorant as others." He is not telling people not to read, but he is telling people not to read indiscriminately, that is to say, reading should be done with careful selection.

Life

"Tin Bucket" 328

— Sun Fushan

What a tin bucket is, I don't need to explain. Look, which household doesn't use a tin bucket? It's really a thing that's so common that there's nothing more to say. How did I get involved with tin buckets? It's a long story. It was in the countryside. Last year, there was a severe drought, and people who had no way to survive heard that it was easy to live in Shanghai, so they all ran to Shanghai. I was one of these famine refugees.

Naturally, standing on the street or pacing back and forth looking at people's faces is not a long-term solution. Therefore, the idea of finding a job came to my mind. Poor relatives also thought I was very smart and spent a lot of effort to ask people to help me get a position as an apprentice in a tin bucket shop. The conditions were: follow the master to work, have food to eat, and get twenty copper coins a month for barber fees. This was only because relatives and friends pleaded in many ways, and the tin bucket boss thought he was doing a good deed before he was willing to take me in.

At first, the boss taught me to hammer the cut tin sheets into a circle with a wooden square. I learned it in less than a few minutes. After a week, he taught me to cut tin sheets. As long as you know how to hold scissors and draw lines on tin sheets, what's so difficult about that! Later, after about a month, he taught me "rolling the edges" and "knocking the bottom." As for "soldering," he never wanted to teach me. I knew he was being sneaky. He was afraid that if I learned it, I would run away. I was really angry. Isn't it easy to learn to make a tin bucket? I learned it all in less than half an hour. I even graduated from a higher elementary school before! One day, the master was not at home, so I secretly made a complete one. I even soldered it, and it didn't leak. It was the same as the master's. I was so happy! Do you know what the master did when he found out later? He cursed, "Damn it! You're very clever!" He looked very impatient and, that night, using an excuse, he gave me a good beating.

In the first few days of entering the shop, I was very happy, but later it was different. The time for making tin buckets is not much, probably seven or eight hours a day, or five or six hours. There are also times when we have to rush to work at night. Then we have to be busy all day and night, until two or three o'clock at night before we can sleep. We call these days "ghosting." When we are not "ghosting," we are just as busy. There are always many things to do. However, we can go to sleep a little earlier. We go to bed at 10:30 at night and have to get up before 6:00 the next morning to empty the chamber pots, sweep the floor, and open the shop door. After working for an hour, we have to make a fire to boil water for the boss and his wife to wash their faces. When I come back from buying vegetables, I also have to start making breakfast. In short, all day long, besides working and cooking, I am holding the child. Although I am still a child myself, I always like children, but I hate the boss's child very much. He is really spoiled. He is more than three years old and still wants people to hold him all day long. He has to eat whatever he wants. If he cries when he is unhappy, the boss's wife will definitely slap me a few times on the face. There is another person in the shop who is suffering like me. He is also fifteen years old and the same "old hand" as me. We two are very close

Page 20

, and we discuss everything before doing it. Their calculations are really shrewd. They won't let me and him go to buy groceries together. They always don't want anyone to be idle.

Probably because I rushed to work at night and got caught in the rain while buying groceries, my "old hand" got sick. At first, they didn't say anything. On the third day, they said, "He's been sick for a long time and is still not getting better. He sleeps and eats and still needs someone to serve him. Tell him to get out!" I was really sad when I heard these words. I thought that we were making "tin buckets," and we were really like a "tin bucket." If a "tin bucket" is rusty and has a hole in it, it will always be thrown aside, and no one will pay attention to it!

After Watching "Peach and Plum Tribulation" 329

— Qingyin

"Peach and Plum Tribulation" can be considered a rather excellent harvest on the film scene recently. This is not only because it has considerable achievements in technology but also because it touches on realistic issues in its content. The fact that this play can move the audience and earn people's tears is not accidental and has its extraordinary qualities.

First of all, we cannot forget the efforts of the stage performers here and the rarity of their achievements. The performance feature of this play is the grand gathering of stage performers making their debut on the silver screen. In fact, from the screenwriter and director to the actors, the stage performers did their jobs and did not ruin their stage. Originally, there is no essential difference between stage acting and silver screen acting. The training and cultivation gained from the stage can also help an actor succeed on the silver screen. The achievements of "Peach and Plum Tribulation" happen to illustrate this fact. The instability of the acting skills of the main actors in "Peach and Plum Tribulation" and the fullness of the emotional process are all gifts from the stage. Although there are not a few places in the performance that are excessive and exaggerated, this may be a small flaw, but in reality, this kind of scene can sometimes obtain unexpected effects. This can be found in "Peach and Plum Tribulation." In many European and American films adapted from stage plays, especially in the famous film "Twentieth Century Express," it is also easy to find this kind of place.

In terms of screenwriting technique, what is worth mentioning is the use of flashbacks and the placement of songs. Starting with the old principal visiting the prison and allowing the story to unfold in the narrative of memories, it appears more tortuous and tasteful than a straightforward narrative and does not fall into mediocrity. The "Graduation Song" is sung during the graduation ceremony only as a necessary part of the story's progress, but when sung in the memory scene of the male protagonist committing a crime and about to be executed, it evokes people's feelings about the fact of "graduation is unemployment." This not only increased the tragic atmosphere of the play but also naturally engraved a painful and profound impression on the audience's eardrums due to the loud voice.

The director is competent. Because this is the first time directing for the silver screen, there are inevitably some shortcomings, such as not grasping the personality of the characters, especially Tao Jianping's personality, clearly enough, and the emotional process sometimes seeming a little too fast, but these are all minor flaws. Isn't he also showing a lot of ability in psychological descriptions and atmosphere?

Finally, what cannot be left unsaid is the not-so-healthy content represented by this play. We cannot deny that the playwright saw reality in his selection of materials, but unfortunately, he did not reasonably explain and reflect this reality. He only saw the surface of reality and did not fundamentally explore the essence of reality. The fact that "graduation is unemployment" is only explained as an accidental phenomenon; it is only because the protagonist Tao Jianping thinks too highly of himself and is unwilling to be patient that he incurs the tragedy and misfortune of unemployment. Assuming that he is able to "be patient," the tide of unemployment will not sweep over him. Isn't this just a fool's dream? In the current social system, it is difficult to allow people to be so optimistic. Assuming that all college and university students can find positions in shipping companies, architects, or labor jobs like Tao Jianping, then the phrase "graduation is unemployment" would be nothing more than a laughable lie. But unfortunately, this phrase accurately represents a serious fact that is difficult to change. This point just illustrates the superficiality of the playwright's understanding of society. But film art should not stay on this superficial level. It should explore the inner layers of things, elucidate the inner nature of things, and indicate the direction of the development of things. Otherwise, some discounts must be given in the evaluation of the entire work. I think "Peach and Plum Tribulation" should be given these discounts because some of its technical achievements are not the achievements of the entire work. — Although it is still a film worth recommending and worth watching.

Current Affairs Research

An Analysis of the Franco-Italian Agreement 330

— Shaomen

After the Great War, the expression of Franco-Italian conflict was almost no less severe than the contradiction between Germany and France. Whether in the Mediterranean, in North Africa, in Central Europe, or in the Balkans, the conflict between France and Italy was clearly expressed. After the Marseilles incident, Yugoslavia, one of France's three satellites, expressed its hatred more clearly and specifically. At the same time, Mussolini did not show weakness and adopted a tough policy towards the South. For a time, the European situation became serious again, with a tendency to have another war. However, before the traces of blood shed by this tragedy had dried, the news that French Foreign Minister Laval had arrived in Rome was spread. Immediately, newspapers all over the world published the news of the signing of the Franco-Italian agreement, "a new page in European history after the European War." At the same time, Yugoslavia, which had harbored hatred, also expressed its attitude of maintaining this agreement together with Romania and Czechoslovakia. This situation is, of course, bound to cause surprise.

Originally, as a result of the European War, France used the Treaty of Versailles to suppress the Germans and dominate Europe, and strongly advocated maintaining the post-war status quo. Not only did Germany desperately oppose this, but Italy also formed the idea of amending the treaty because the status quo created by this treaty was unfavorable to it. However, after Hitler came to power, on the one hand, he greatly threatened France because of his high-profile call for rearmament and the abolition of the treaty. On the other hand, he actively carried out the merger of Austria, which made Italy feel deeply uneasy. In this situation, in order to maintain its post-war spoils of victory, France worked hard to ease the conflict between France and Italy in order to stop Germany's attempt to break the contract. As for Italy, it also wanted to maintain its existing position and development path in Central Europe and did not want the merger of Germany and Austria to become a reality. For a time, it also wanted to unite France to deal with the Germans. Although the contradictions between France and Italy are very complex and sharp, they are constantly trying to conditionally ease their contradictions to seek temporary compromise on a certain shared interest. The Franco-Italian agreement recently signed in Rome is a manifestation of the fact that France and Italy, under the unstable trend of Germany's foreign policy, are mutually easing their contradictions and seeking temporary compromises with various conditions.

According to reports, the Franco-Italian agreement is divided into four parts, and the main content is as follows:

1. France agrees to cede 114,000 square kilometers of land south of Italian Libya to Libya; and to cede the coastline opposite the Bab-el-Mandeb Strait under the jurisdiction of French Somaliland to Italian Eritrea. ...

2. Italy may participate in the operation of the railway from French Djibouti to Addis Ababa, the capital of Abyssinia.

3. France and Italy jointly propose that all neighboring countries of Austria and Austria should mutually conclude an agreement of non-interference and non-aggression. France, Poland, and Romania may also join the agreement, so that when the territorial integrity of Austria is threatened, all countries may hold consultations with Austria. ...

4. Regarding the issue of equality of armament rights, the French and Italian governments, based on the declaration of the five powers of Britain, the United States, France, Germany, and Italy on December 11, 1932, jointly recognize that no country

After Seeing the Performance of the Leng Yan Dance Troupe 331

— Ping Yao

After touring several ports like Beiping, Tianjin, and Qingdao, the Leng Yan Dance Troupe has now arrived in Shanghai. They have already performed in several cinemas, including the Southeast, Huade, and Empire. Their performance this time represents another trend in the dance world, which is that they do not appeal to the audience with sensuality, but devote all their efforts to the technical aspects of the dance itself. This is a noteworthy point.

Speaking of technique, there is much to mention in terms of singing, dancing, and music. Miss Louise, the former leading figure of the "Xiaying" Dance Troupe and now a key member of Leng Yan, is gifted with a beautiful voice, and her "solo" is enough to attract attention. In terms of dance, the troupe hired a Russian dance teacher in Tianjin for a long period of instruction, so their performances can be described as skilled, and the dance postures also have a foreign flavor. Programs such as "Cossack Dance," "Russian Court Dance," "Tango," "Gypsy Dance," "French Dance," etc., mostly represent a national character and also have a kind of healthy and powerful dance posture, which are quite eye-catching. In terms of music, the troupe's orchestra is relatively well-organized, and the seven members are mostly well-versed in music, so the results are no less than those of Shanghai's dance troupes. In addition, the drama "By Hook or by Crook" (this play has been performed many times in Shanghai), starring Ms. Liu Mang and Louise from the troupe, although the scenery is inevitably a bit simple, the acting skills of the two are quite remarkable. As for the outdated content of this play, that is another matter, and I will not discuss it here.

Finally, I would like to say something about my hopes for the troupe. The troupe has already seen the need to change the trend of song and dance, but I am afraid that they have not paid enough attention to the need for new creations in song and dance. Imitating others is never enough. They should have artistic, audience-pleasing, healthy and powerful new creations in order to meet the needs of the vast audience. Otherwise, it will be difficult to achieve success in business, and it will also be difficult to have any performance in the development of song and dance art itself. I wonder if the gentlemen of the troupe agree with my humble opinion?

Page 21

Unilaterally changing the obligations regarding armaments; regarding this issue, when necessary, the two governments may consult with each other.

This clearly shows that: on the one hand, France ceded some land and rights in African colonies to Italy, to satisfy its eagerness to expand its African colonies to a considerable extent; at the same time, France and its satellite Little Entente countries jointly guaranteed Austria's independence and prevented the German-Austrian merger, in order to maintain its access to the Balkans through Austria; on the other hand, Italy did not harass Yugoslavia, did not harm France's interests in the Balkans, and jointly maintained Austria's independence and European peace with France and the Little Entente (that is, jointly maintained the status quo in Europe), in order to protect some of the effects of the Treaty of Versailles, which had long been torn up, so that the benefits France gained in the Great War could be preserved. - The so-called Franco-Italian agreement was established under such conditions. Its primary function, of course, was to ease the conflict between France and Italy and to jointly monitor Germany on a certain point.

However, post-war Germany had to find a way out. In the meantime, Germany had only two paths to take: one was to realize the German-Austrian merger and compete with France and Italy to gain access to the Balkans; the other was to head north to the Baltic Sea and invade the Soviet Union to the east. But recent facts have shown that the former path is greatly hindered and not easy to follow, forcing it to shift its gaze entirely to the east and take the latter path. For example, Germany's befriending of Poland, Hitler's deletion of anti-French phrases from his autobiography, the repeated publication of "peace" speeches by National Socialists, and the reunion of German and French veterans are all obvious examples of this German tendency. What about France? Naturally, it wants to guarantee its own "security" and prevent Germany from rising up to take revenge, but if Germany really does not take the westward route and goes straight to the east, it will also agree. The problem here is that France cannot believe that Germany has really abandoned its revengeful intentions and will not attack Paris. If it can get the support of Italy and even Britain in Europe to jointly monitor Germany's implementation of its eastward policy, then French imperialism can hide from its enemies with powerful help and make them fight with others. What's wrong with that for it? Originally, France's approach to Germany was nothing more than one of these two: before Germany recovered its vitality, it would launch a defensive war against Germany to prevent it from rising again; it hoped that Germany would move east and avoid direct conflict between Germany and France. But the former is very dangerous because it cannot get the support of Britain and Italy; the latter is easier to get the support and guarantee of Britain and Italy, but it is very "safe". Therefore, as long as possible, France will of course adopt the latter policy. The recently signed Franco-Italian agreement, in addition to being used by France and Italy to monitor Germany and prevent it from harming their interests, also has the implication of making Germany's outward path from west to east: this is of course the result of British and French diplomatic policy. The Soviet Union's "Izvestia" newspaper agreed with the British newspaper's analysis of this issue, saying: "The Rome talks, as the British newspaper said, will be an expression of creating some favorable conditions for building a bridge between Germany and France. British diplomats are working in this direction. This is nothing more than obtaining an appropriate level of rhetoric and documents from the German side and allowing Germany's legal right to expand its military." Although there are no provisions in the published Franco-Italian agreement to allow Germany to rearm, we believe that France, Italy and even Britain must have concrete discussions on this issue. For example, British Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to France before the event, Britain's expression of joy afterwards, the French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister's visit to London, Laval's plan to visit Berlin, France's recent indifference to the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, the British openly advocating the abolition of military clauses in the peace treaty, the "resurrection" of the dead disarmament conference, the widespread rumors of Germany's return to disarmament in Europe and the United States... - All of these reveal another function of the Rome Agreement: "to create some favorable conditions for building a bridge between France and Germany", "to allow Germany's legal right to expand its military", so that it can move east.

However, long nights are fraught with dreams, and whether the development of all events is as planned by the European powers is still a question worth studying.

Amateur Coffee Shop

Reality and Hope 332

— Fei Peng

Hope and reality are the two vitalities of human survival. No matter how reality makes you unfulfilled, makes you bored, and disappointed, you still cannot suddenly leave it, no matter how bad it is. Because people are already living in reality, there is absolutely no reason to live completely without reality. Reality is something that humans cannot get rid of. Wearing clothes, eating, living in houses, making friends, having sex, doing what you are doing and want to do, and saying what you are saying and want to say are all reality. Everyone lives in this reality, and everyone's life is expressed as their own personal reality. Without reality, there is no life.

Although reality is the content of every person's life and the conditions of life, the reality of any era and any individual will make him unable to be satisfied, so he cannot but have another kind of hope as the driving force of life. Otherwise, not only will mankind not be able to progress, but even the existing reality will not be able to be maintained, and life will not be able to continue. Because no matter whether a person's hope can become a reality in the future, he always needs to have a hope to succeed, and he already has a hope. A person who has the highest power, even if he has climbed to the highest spire of the pyramid-shaped organization of human society, still has his future hopes. Therefore, ancient emperors such as Qin Shi Huang and Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty still hoped to live forever and sent people to the sea or built terraces to seek immortals. Other holders of the highest power hope that they can permanently maintain their position without being shaken. Merchants certainly hope to recover their capital after losing money, and even those who have made money hope to make more money. Workers hope to get a raise tomorrow and have more income in a month. Farmers hope that next year's harvest will be better than this year's. People who write articles hope that the稿費 is higher and that every article can be sold. Women who find a husband also hope to give birth to a son early, marry a daughter-in-law, and have grandchildren. In short, a lot of future life aspirations become everyone's hopes and fantasies, and linger in their minds, forming a part of their lives and lives. Hope, simply put, is mankind's desire to comfort itself and make up for the shortcomings of reality in the midst of dissatisfaction with reality. When people have a hope, they can comfort themselves and continue to live. Hope is looking forward to the future, but it increases mankind's fighting spirit and courage. Mankind must have hope, must have the future aspirations that lure him, and then he can move forward. Mankind's progress is here, and the burning and driving force of life are also here. If mankind had no hope, I am afraid that he would have stayed in primitive society and would not have been able to move forward. If an individual does not have a hope to burn his heart and become a disappointed person, then he will definitely come to the future of suicide!

From this point of view, hope and reality are contradictory and harmonious. Because without reality, you would have already ceased to exist, so where would there be any hope? Without hope, you cannot live to enjoy reality and continue to create reality, and all existing and future realities will disappear in your disappointment. And on the one hand, only reality gives you experience, so that you can feel satisfied or disgusted, and thus have hope. On the other hand, only hope can make you create continuous reality and create it as your reality in the continuation of life. However, reality and hope are also contradictory. Because without dissatisfaction with reality, you would not have hope and move towards the future that you grasp, which means that you abandon reality. Conversely, if you are content with the satisfaction of reality and grasp it and are unwilling to give it up, it means that you have no other hope and have abandoned the future. In other words, you are completely standing on reality and are unwilling to leave it even one step, so there is no need for hope, hope disappears, and reality negates hope in this way. Just like completely fantasizing about the hope of the future, or simply not talking about reality, then you have no content of life and no possibility of survival, reality disappears, and hope also negates reality in this way. Reality wants you to stay in its arms and does not allow you to leave, but hope wants you to leave reality and run forward with it, so they contradict and negate each other in this way. Because of this, a proper life is often stepping on two boats: you must grasp reality and also establish hope and pursue the future. The harmony of reality and hope is in maintaining your life, and the contradiction of reality and hope is also in creating your life. People live in contradiction, contradiction is the stream of life, and it is also the torch that guides life.

However, there are two strange people in the world: one kind of people specializes in teaching people to be content with reality, saying that you should not be dissatisfied with reality and oppose it, your hope is a fantasy, do not leave reality and tend to fantasy, you should abandon hope, abandon fantasy and completely obey the arrangements of reality. Reality tells you how to live, and you should live like that, even if you suffer deeply in reality, you must live like this, and resisting reality is a sin. But they do not know that without dissatisfaction, boredom, resistance, and abandonment of real life, you will not be able to yearn for the future and have hope, and use it as your driving force. In this way, mankind will not evolve, and individuals will become passive or even commit suicide due to disappointment. There is also a kind of person who specializes in teaching people to hope for the future, especially religious people. They say that reality is indeed painful, but you should completely forget the pain of reality, endure the teasing of reality, and hope for future compensation. This is completely taking the hope of the future as a hypnotic, a way to hypnotize patients to make them forget the pain of disease, and this method also does not allow people to oppose reality. They do not know that completely ignoring reality and hoping for the future is to make people immediately lose the basis of survival, and after making people lose the foothold of reality, they cannot create the future and achieve hope. Obviously, for example, eating and wearing clothes are reality. If there is no food to eat and no clothes to wear, people will starve to death and freeze to death. What future can there be to hope for?

In short, mankind does not only live in the present, nor is the present life the perfect end. He also has to live in the future, live in a more perfect life. Therefore, he should live in reality, and he should also live in hope. You must be dissatisfied with reality to have hope, and you must be able to live in reality to create the future and realize your hope. You must have reality and also the hope of the future, you must resist reality and also not specialize in fantasizing about the future. This may seem contradictory, but this contradiction is the law of human life and also the law of human historical evolution.

Introduction to "Volcano" 333

— Liu Xin

—Published by Shanghai Magazine Company—

Since the May Fourth Movement, the form of poetry has been liberated, but what has been achieved other than the early hastily written articles?

Our poetry world is extremely silent. When we only look back at those majestic poems originating in Northern Europe, the warm songs of Western Europe, and the delicate and蕴藉诽句 of the island country, we cannot help but feel sad about the decline and depravity of our national spirit. Poetry is the voice of the soul of a nation. It will shout out the emotions of the masses' suffering, and it will praise the unique spirit of a nation. However, our poetry world is so silent that there is almost no movement.

China is a land not suitable for cultural workers to grow. Just look at the thinness and even abuse of the society towards intellectuals in recent years, and you can already understand this tragic fact. The poet Zhu Xiang committed suicide by throwing himself into the river, and Peng Jiahuan passed away in days of poverty and illness. The general decline in cultural standards, the general weakness of readers' purchasing power, and the publishing industry have also been flooded with the angry tide of depression since 1933. New books are estimated at one yuan for three pounds, and articles are priced at one yuan per thousand words; when a poet is born in this era, who will care about his lines of poetry? The silence of the poetry world is one reason.

Amateur Entertainment

Playing with Lanterns 334

— Tao Ren

In Guizhou, during the New Year, the happiest, most lively and most interesting thing is probably "playing with lanterns." There are several kinds of lanterns, such as "dragon lanterns," "lion lanterns," "flower lanterns," "cart lanterns," and so on. This is almost enthusiastically held in any county or village in Guizhou. There are two meanings to "playing with lanterns": one is to celebrate the New Year and join in the fun, and the other is that these "lanterns" each represent a god, and the responsibility of these gods is to "keep the streets clean and protect the peace of the four seas."

Playing with "dragon lanterns" is an extremely grand ritual. The dragon is shaped with bamboo strips, pasted with paper, and then painted with the colorful stripes that the so-called dragon should have. The dragon coat is made of cloth, and the body is twelve or fifteen sections long. The dragon comes out from the ninth to the fifteenth day of the New Year. In front of the dragon, there are several rows of lanterns, tied into strange shapes of shrimp soldiers, crab generals, and aquatic creatures, and there are also eight immortals tied up separately. Then, amid the sound of gongs and drums, the "dragon lantern" appears. Playing with the dragon is playing with "fireworks." You only see the "dragon lantern" rolling in the flames, and the "fireworks" also have many tricks. Some of them are released in blue, some in white, and some in red. When people make "fireworks," they either put a layer of paper in the middle to make them suddenly interrupt when they are released with full force, or they put a little "tide nao" in the gunpowder to make them make a loud roar when they are released, almost like they are about to explode. Under these many embellishments, the "dragon" of the "dragon lantern" really seems to appear vividly, with the ambition to travel thousands of miles. The audience is blocked on the way, and often causes many disputes because the "dragon handle" hurts people.

"Playing with lions" is in the daytime, and you can see it as early as the second day of the New Year. Playing with "ground lions" is nothing, but just performing all the living habits of the lion. But the "stage lion" is really amazing. "Crossing the corner" and "passing through the stage" are not uncommon. What makes people shudder the most is climbing a high platform made of forty-one or seventy-one benches, and still doing many plays on it, and the stage is trembling and almost about to fall down. You can play up from below, and you can play down from above. In addition to the lion, there is also a "smiling arhat" and a "Sun Wukong." It is the responsibility of "Sun Wukong" to dismantle the benches one by one at the top, and he always has to do a somersault or lift a tripod on each bench. Oh, I forgot to tell you how the lion is made. The lion's head is made of cardboard, with nine colors and bells on its head, and the mouth is movable. The body is made of cloth cut into a round, arc-shaped shape and connected to the head. Two people put on the lion's mask, one playing the head and the other playing the tail. Human feet are equal to the four feet of the lion. Here I have to praise my several "old cousins." Their playing is purely skilled. If you are building a new house and want a lion to step on the beam, they can put on spiked shoes (extremely slippery on wood and very heavy) and roll, turn, and turn their heads on the beam without showing any flaws.

"Flower lanterns" and "cart lanterns" are relatively plain, but they also have their low-level fun. The protagonists of both types of lanterns are a girl and a clown, also called "Dou Meimei." They say and sing, and they can say anything nonsense; however, there must also be a system and a story. They have to go to people's houses to play with lanterns. If they encounter a closed door, it will be troublesome, and they have to play "connecting words"; if both sides are experts, they can really talk eloquently and talk for two or three hours, from "how many stars are in the sky" to "why play with lanterns" and "please open the door for wealth for the host," they should be eloquent and not pause, otherwise, they will lose face. This is also from the ninth day of the New Year to the fifteenth day. The difference between "cart lanterns" and "flower lanterns" is that the Meimei of the "cart lanterns" is always in the paper-pasted cart box and cannot get off the ground, and cannot enter the hall of people's houses, because it represents the smallest god, said to be a parturient woman.

Page 22

Page 23

However, in this vast area, there are still people who work hard and diligently. The "Volcano" poetry magazine finally appeared before us in a brand-new posture at the end of 1934, thanks to the struggle of a few young poets.

This event will become a miracle of 1935.

I read her inaugural issue on a quiet midnight. After reading it, my mind was filled with pictures of human suffering. She sang:

They fell by themselves without wind

Falling on a dusty pillow

On a brownish-gold old cotton robe

On an opened book page

The parasol tree shed her crimson little boat

And from the top of my tree

Falling long threadlike leaves one by one

These fallen leaves

Falling from the top of my tree

—Louis's "Hair"

Louis's works have made many contributions to "Modern" in the past. Although his lyric poems are covered with a thick fog of sadness, his delicate brushstrokes and melancholic tones are his unique style.

Heaven

Drip your blue nectar in my eyes

Sprinkle your blue fragrant powder on my head

Ah, lovely October day

Turn your blue soft waves

Lift the blue long skirt of your young girl

XXXX

You cover me with infinite mysterious blue

Cover the parasol tree and the earth

XXXX

Blue hypnotic song

I gradually close my drunken eyes

Shaking non-stop

Her golden shoulders

This gray and silent earth

The crows came

Singing a black song

On the pieces of fallen leaves

Weighing down suffocating dreams

A tired and heavy heart

This is the miserable cry of us who are confined in the iron barrel of labor and sorrow all day long, vented from the low beat by the poet's beautifying pen.

There is no need to cite more such examples. In short, after reading this kind of poem, although the heart feels infinitely heavy, the body gets infinite comfort instead, as if the limbs and bones are all crisp and scattered.

Louis, Ding Xin, Lao Mai, etc. in "Volcano" are all promising young and enthusiastic poets. I hope that in addition to self-encouragement in hardship, they must also enrich their own life experiences, find new paths for new poetry, and hope that society will no longer cruelly destroy this newly planted fresh flower. When I wrote this article, my heart was filled with so many hopes!

Biographies of Famous People

Biography of Einstein (1) 338

— From Mu

Albert Einstein is a world-renowned revolutionary in modern science. The emergence of his "theory of relativity" not only overturned the famous Newtonian mechanics that had dominated science for over two hundred years, throwing a powerful bomb into physics and the entire natural sciences, but also had a tremendous impact on modern philosophy and modern thought, forcing various idealistic theories and mysterious mechanical ideas to further expose their fallacies. Therefore, we can say that those who do not know Einstein's scholarship and life cannot fully understand the changes and development of modern science, philosophy, and thought.

I have not yet seen any systematic works on Einstein's biography and scholarship in our publishing industry. I am now introducing Einstein to everyone based on the recently published Japanese book "Biography of Einstein" (written by Kuwaki Otohiko); however, this is a rather large book, and I cannot translate it in its entirety to publish as an article. Therefore, I can only briefly compile a "Biography of Einstein" based on this book. If this can enable everyone to have a considerable understanding of this great modern scientist—Einstein—then it will not be in vain.

(I)

Einstein was born on March 14, 1879, in the city of Ulm in southern Germany. This place is located on the left bank of the upper reaches of the Danube, which flows through Germany and Austria, and has always been an important transportation hub. Five or six hundred years ago, a large Gothic monastery was built here, with a spire 161 meters high, which is the tallest monastery building in the world. Einstein is considered to have reached the highest peak in the history of world science, and he was born in a place with the world's tallest monastery building. Isn't that interesting?

Six years after Einstein's birth, his family moved to Munich, where he spent his childhood.

When Einstein was only four or five years old, his father gave him a small compass to play with. At that time, he had an inexplicable feeling about the movement of the magnetic needle in the compass. Even after his father explained it, he still could not explain his surprise. Also, at that time, a cousin of his came from Genoa and talked about the land, people, harbors, ships, etc. of Italy. After listening to it, he was first amazed by the vastness of the world, and then he took an old box from his father's workshop to imitate a sailing game—although this cannot be regarded as a sign of his becoming a great scientist, his character and achievements are somewhat related to it.

However, due to the stimulation of these things, due to his feeling of the inexplicability and vastness of nature, he was led to a pantheistic religious heart that unified nature and God. His father, influenced by the utilitarian ideas of the time, was a free thinker who did not value religion and did not perform Jewish rituals in his own family. However, he hoped that Einstein would strictly abide by Jewish rules.

When he turned six, Einstein went to elementary school. However, at that time, he deeply felt dissatisfied with the rules of the elementary school he was in, the school's facilities, and the unequal treatment of rich and poor children in the school. At the same time, because he was Jewish, he began to suffer from anti-Semitism in his elementary school life.

Einstein loved art since he was a child, especially music. His mother also played the piano and liked classical things. He started learning the violin at the age of six, so when he became an adult, his musical knowledge had a considerable foundation.

His secondary education was also received in Munich. The school he attended was a secondary school that mainly implemented classical education in Greek and Latin. However, his impression of this secondary school was the same as his impression of the elementary school he attended: a mechanical school that implemented soulless education. However, there was a teacher there named Louis who distributed some lectures on Greek, Roman, and classical German literature, which aroused his interest in classical literature. According to what he said at the age of thirty, two or three years after he had published his first paper on relativity and his name had been noticed by some people in the academic community, he had specially visited this old teacher; but this teacher had never remembered him, and instead looked at him strangely as to why he came to visit, so he felt greatly disillusioned and hurriedly left.

In his youth, Einstein showed early maturity in mathematical talent. At the age of thirteen, he had already learned the elementary geometry textbook ahead of the school curriculum. However, he was different from Young and Hamilton; these two were not only precocious scientists, but also precocious in linguistic talent. Although Einstein's mathematical talent showed amazing precocity, his linguistic skills were very mediocre. He had failed an exam because his grades in language and natural history were too bad.

Einstein also liked philosophy books very much. Bichner's "Force and Matter," which was popular at the time, gave him a deep impression. He increasingly approached materialistic monism, but the religious psychology he had since childhood had not been completely eliminated; in his school, there was also Jewish education, and teachers Dr. Tochter and Borlai gave him unforgettable religious inspiration.

When he was about to graduate from secondary school, a major change occurred in his family. The electrical business run by his father failed, forcing his family to leave Munich and move to Italy, but Einstein had to stay in Munich until he graduated.

Einstein had no interest in his father's business and never went to his father's factory. He also had no interest in the life of the Munich streets. He was only thinking about Italy, because he had heard some things about Italy from his cousin who came from Genoa, and he thought that Italy was the paradise of this world; and his parents were in this paradise at that time, and in their correspondence, they made him imagine how bright and free Italy was. One day, he quickly went to his parents' side. Because he really wanted to go to Italy, he asked a doctor for a leave of absence certificate with the reason of neurasthenia without waiting for graduation. Since then, for half a year, he completely left school life. Under the bright sun, in the colorful scenery of northern Italy, he socialized with the free young people of Milan.
